# Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") |
| Location(s): | [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn"), [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") |
| Reward: | None |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =3 (Delphine) |
| ID: | MQ106 |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller") | **Next →** [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") | | |

Alduin resurrecting Sahloknir

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine").
2. Locate the dragon burial site.
3. Kill the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
4. Talk to Delphine.

### A Harmless Innkeeper

Now that you know that the [Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:Horn of Jurgen Windcaller") has been pilfered from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav"), follow the instructions in the [mysterious note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(Delphine) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (Delphine)") left in its place. This will lead you to [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") and the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn"). Speak with the innkeeper, [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine"), about renting the attic room. She will tell you that there is no such room, but you can take the room on the left. Delphine will follow you to the sparse room she indicated, where she will address you as Dragonborn and give you the Horn. She cryptically tells you that you and she need to talk and asks you to follow her.

### The Problem with Dragons

Delphine will lead you to a room across the inn. She will ask you to close the door to the room before both you and she can proceed any further. Do it, and she will open a secret passage in the back of a wardrobe that leads down to a subterranean room.

Here Delphine will reveal that she took the Horn to attract the attention of the Dragonborn. The note was a safeguard to protect against trickery by the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"). She also tells you that the dragons are not just coming back, but are actually coming back to life, resurrected from their burial mounds. Only the Dragonborn can permanently kill dragons by absorbing their souls. But she is not quite ready to accept you as Dragonborn, despite the [Greybeards'](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") interest in you. Luckily, she has a task to prove your authenticity. According to the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone") map taken from [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"), the next dragon will rise from a burial mound in [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"). She wants you to accompany her to the burial site and kill the dragon; only then will she accept you as Dragonborn.

If you tell her you're ready to leave, she will put on her gear and leave the inn. You are free to follow Delphine to Kynesgrove, and she will briefly talk to you at waypoints about her concerns. Or you can go at your own pace and possibly beat her there.

### Kynesgrove

As soon as you get to Kynesgrove, [Iddra](/wiki/Skyrim:Iddra "Skyrim:Iddra"), the innkeeper, will run up to you and tell you that a dragon was sighted flying over the burial mound and that you should get out of town. If you traveled with Delphine, she will run up ahead of you to the burial mound, fearing it may be too late. If you arrived ahead of her, she will appear shortly thereafter on the mound behind you.

### Speaking with Dragons

Upon arriving at the site, you and Delphine will witness the dragon, [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin"), using his [Thu'um](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") to resurrect a dead dragon. Alduin cannot be killed or injured at this time. When the dragon, [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir"), is whole once more, he has a conversation in the [dragon language](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Language "Lore:Dragon Language") with Alduin.

- Alduin: *Sahloknir, ziil gro dovah ulse!*
  - Sahloknir! Your soul is bound to me for eternity!
- Alduin: *Slen tiid vo!*
  - (Flesh Time Opposite Of)
- Sahloknir: *Alduin, thuri! Boaan tiid vokriiha suleyksejun kruziik?*
  - Alduin, my king (overlord)! Has the time arrived (flown) to restore (unkill) your ancient dominion (power-of-king)?
- Alduin: *Geh, Sahloknir, kaali mir.*
  - Yes, Sahloknir, my loyal champion. Start with these mortals.

Here, Alduin attempts to speak to you, addressing you as [Dovahkiin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin").

- Alduin: *Ful, losei Dovahkiin? Zu'u koraav nid nol dov do hi.*
  - So, you're the Dragonborn? I see nothing of the dragon about you. (So, you are Dragonborn? I recognize no from dragon of you.)
- Alduin: *You do not even know our tongue, do you? Such arrogance, to dare take for yourself the name of Dovah.*
- Alduin: *Sahloknir, krii daar joorre.*
  - Sahloknir, kill these mortals.

After ordering Sahloknir to kill you, Alduin flies away. Delphine will help you kill Sahloknir, and upon his death, when you absorb his soul, Delphine will be quick to acknowledge you as Dragonborn.

### Paranoia

Speak to her, and she will reveal that she is one of the last members of the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"). She will also tell you about her suspicions that the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") are responsible for the return of the dragons. Since the Thalmor are part of the [Aldmeri Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion") and nearly destroyed the Empire during the [Great War](/wiki/Lore:Great_War "Lore:Great War") only 30 years ago, they have a motive for rescuing [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") in [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), simply in order to keep the war raging. The Thalmor stand to benefit most from damage to the Empire by the dragons.

Finally, she will reveal her plan to infiltrate the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") to search for evidence of their connection with the dragons. She has no idea how to get past embassy security, and asks you to meet her back in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). This quest concludes, and the [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") quest starts.

## Notes

- While A Blade in the Dark is active, random dragon encounters are eliminated, and dragon locations will be limited to [Dragon Lairs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"), allowing for controlled access to dragon fights.
- Despite it saying you need gold to rent the "attic room" (and Delphine taking said gold if you do), you do not actually need the gold on you to progress the quest.
- When Delphine goes to put her traveling gear on at the start of the quest in Riverwood, she will stand next to the chest, although the chest beforehand states that it is empty.
- Delphine will not acknowledge your status as Dragonborn if you slay a dragon that is not Sahloknir, despite any soul absorption.
- You can happen upon the burial site any time after Delphine leaves Riverwood. The quest will progress once you arrive.
- Standing too close to the burial mound when Alduin revives Sahloknir may cause you to be thrown aside in a manner similar to the Unrelenting Force shout. Though you can likely pick yourself back up before Alduin's and Sahloknir's conversation ends and the battle begins, you can be thrown off the hill and take fall damage, so be careful.
- The other named NPCs of Kynesgrove will all take shelter in [Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine") while the dragons are present. You can check in on them on your way up the hill from the inn and speak to them to hear quest-specific dialogue.
- If you rent a regular room at the Sleeping Giant first, then ask for the attic room, Delphine will comment on this, with "Why didn't you say so the first time?"
- If you have married either [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver") or [Roggi Knot-Beard](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggi_Knot-Beard "Skyrim:Roggi Knot-Beard") (providing Roggi is not your active follower) and moved them to another house before starting this quest, they will be teleported to Steamscorch Mine as soon as A Blade in the Dark is started, and will remain there until it is completed.
- If the *[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")* add-on is installed and the quest [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha") isn't done yet, you may not be able to absorb the dragon soul after killing it (as [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") wishes steal it). If he does absorb the dragon soul, Delphine may still give you credit for it.
  -  You can use the commands `setstage MQ106 155`, and `setstage MQ106 160`, and then speak to Delphine. Once the quest is finished, fast travel to Kynesgrove before walking back to the dragon skeleton to see the Miraak soul theft animation.

## Bugs

- After renting the "attic room", Delphine may enter your room but not speak, breaking the rest of the quest.
  - Make sure you have shut the door behind you before talking to Delphine - she asks you to do this.
  -  This can be fixed by typing `setstage mq106 30` in the console, depositing the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller in your inventory and skipping to Delphine's 'we need to talk' dialogue.
- Sometimes when you reach the dragon burial mound, Sahloknir will not fully emerge from the ground, and does not die when his health reaches zero.
- If you kill Sahloknir before he gets his skin the quest is broken **?**
  - This can be fixed by walking far enough out of the dragon's range, which extends as far as Kynesgrove, and walking back.
- Talking to Delphine after slaying Sahloknir and absorbing his soul may not trigger the quest update.
  - This can be fixed by reloading a save and before going to Kynesgrove, make sure to first complete the "Horn of Jurgen Windcaller" Quest by going to the Grey Beards and returning the Horn to them. Also, make sure that you have learned the shout "Become Ethereal" in Ustengrav, and activated the altar where you found the note from Delphine to gain a Dragon Soul. Use that Dragon Soul to activate "Become Ethereal". Then go meet Delphine in Kynesgrove and slay the Dragon.
  - Uninstall/Disable the mod "View Yourself VR" if you have it, because it has been reported to cause this bug.
  -  Using the console command `SetObjectiveCompleted MQ106 40 1` can correct this so that the player will progress to the point where Delphine will offer to tell all.
  -  Using the console command `setstage MQ106 155` can correct this. Follow up with `setstage MQ106 160`.
  -  If Delphine is still not responding, the main questline can be forwarded to the beginning of the [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") quest by using `completequest MQ106` followed by `setstage MQ201 30`. This will cause Delphine to run back to the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), where her dialogue will be reset for the new quest. It will also add [Delphine's Secret Door Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine%27s_Secret_Door_Key "Skyrim:Delphine's Secret Door Key") to your inventory.
  -  If this also doesn't work, you can load your last saved game, slay Sahloknir, absorb the soul and then move very slowly to Delphine. Don't talk to her, wait until she finished all her lines and repeats the last one - then talk to her.
- Sometimes, you may not be able to absorb the dragon soul until you complete the quest. **?**
- Sometimes, when Sahloknir emerges he may have his skin already attached. The effect of his skin returning still plays.
- On Xbox One and PS4, while traveling with Delphine when you reach [Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers"), Delphine will notice and comment about the bandit place if you had not raided it yet, and she will immediately disappear. **?**
- She will appear about 100 meters up the path. **?**
- If Roggi Knot-Beard is your follower when Delphine tells you about the impending Kynesgrove dragon attack, he may cower and say lines as though he were hiding in Steamscorch Mine with the other Kynesgrove residents, although he will still leave the Sleeping Giant of his own accord and run in the direction of home. **?**
- After you finish the quest, Kynesgrove guards may comment on a dragon attack there as though it took place somewhere else.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| A Blade in the Dark (MQ106) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 30 |  | Delphine, the innkeeper in Riverwood, is more than she seems. She was the one that left me the note in Ustengrav. She gave me back the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller. She went to a lot of trouble to get my attention. I should find out what she wants. *Objective 10:* Talk to Delphine |
| 50 |  | Delphine believes that dragons are coming back to life and that the next one will resurrect near the town of Kynesgrove. Once I've convinced her that I'm Dragonborn by killing the dragon, she promises to fully explain who she is and what she wants with me. *Objective 20:* Locate the dragon burial site |
| 102 |  | *Objective 30:* Kill the dragon Sahloknir |
| 150 |  | Delphine believes that dragons are coming back to life and that only the Dragonborn can stop them. Near Kynesgrove, we saw a dragon Shouting another one back to life. That dragon is dead, and now it's time for Delphine to give me some answers. *Objective 40:* Talk to Delphine |
| 200 | ☑ | Delphine believes that dragons are coming back to life and that only the Dragonborn can stop them. It turns out that she was right. Near Kynesgrove, we saw a dragon Shouting another one back to life. After we killed the dragon and I absorbed its power, Delphine accepted that I was Dragonborn as she had hoped, and revealed that she is one of the last members of the Blades, an organization dedicated to protecting the Dragonborn and stopping the dragons. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 5, 10, 20, 25, 32, 35, 40, 42, 45, 47, 48, 55, 58, 60, 65, 70, 72, 75, 80, 90, 100, 105, 110, 120, 155, 160, 170.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ106 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ106`.

# Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Help teach [a merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei") to mind his own business.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | 100 Gold |
| ID: | TG00 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business") | | |

Brynjolf trying to sell his elixir

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf").
2. Steal [Madesi's Silver Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi%27s_Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Madesi's Silver Ring").
3. Plant Madesi's Silver Ring *or* drop Madesi's Ring and speak to Brynjolf.
4. Speak to Brynjolf.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When you come across a merchant named [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") at the [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") bazaar during the day or in [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") at night, he will propose that you frame a vendor by planting a stolen ring on his person. The intended victim, [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei"), has apparently become aware that someone is doing something wrong, and that someone wants him in jail where he can't interfere.

If you accept, Brynjolf will tell you that he will create a distraction in the bazaar. While this draws people's attention, you are to steal a ring from [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi"). Madesi keeps the ring in a strongbox inside the cabinet under the counter of his stall, both of which are locked. You can unlock the cabinet and strongbox at night for an easier theft, or simply pickpocket Madesi's key off of him. Then, wait until after 4pm to actually steal the ring. Note that the ring you must steal will specifically say "Madesi's Silver Ring," rather than just any silver ring.

After stealing the ring, sneak up to Brand-Shei and position yourself behind the crates he is sitting on. [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket#2 "Skyrim:Pickpocket") him and place the ring in his inventory. If you wish to spare Brand-Shei, you can drop the ring instead and tell Brynjolf you lost it. He won't be very happy, but you will be able to proceed to the next quest nonetheless.

This quest can also be completed without stealing and pickpocketing by simply waiting while Brynjolf distracts the crowd. If you do attempt the theft and are caught by a wandering guard, you will be arrested. In either case, you will still be able to progress to the next quest.

Speak to Brynjolf to receive a reward of 100 septims and a chance to join the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

## Notes

- No matter what you do, Brynjolf will still approach you, meaning that if you do not intend to do the Thieves Guild, the quest will always be in your journal.
  - Using the forge next to the market before Brynjolf approaches you will cause him to ask you his opening question a few times while you are in the smithing animation and then walk away, after which he will not approach you again, which will prevent the quest from being added to your journal.
- As soon as Brynjolf informs you of his plan you will receive a hidden perk increasing your pickpocketing chances by 30%, which makes planting the ring significantly easier. The perk will be removed once the quest is complete.
- If you are caught, Madesi's Silver Ring can be found afterwards in the evidence chest in Riften Jail.
- After this quest is completed successfully, you may find Brand-Shei in the castle dungeon. You can talk to him and receive his [identity quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Distant_Memories "Skyrim:Distant Memories") from there if you did not receive it before.
- After this quest is completed, there is a 20% chance of encountering a thief in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") and [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

## Bugs

- Leaving Riften during this quest could prevent the quest from progressing.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Brand-Shei becomes imprisoned in Riften Jail forever, instead of just for a week.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  -  Fixed by entering the following in the console: `set TG00BrandSheiJail to 0`. The next time Brand-Shei's schedule is updated, he will leave jail and resume his original schedule. Force him to update his schedule right away by selecting him in the console (or entering `prid 19DDC`) and then entering `evp`.
- If you speak to Maul after speaking to Brynjolf and pick the conversational option *"Know anything about the Thieves Guild?"*, the miscellaneous quest *"Talk to Brynjolf about joining the Thieves Guild"* may become stuck in your quest list.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  -  In the console, enter `setstage TG00MaulHandler 200` to remove the entry.
- Brynjolf can comment about you sniffing out his scheme at the north Riften gate even if you never actually entered the city that way.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- If you steal Madesi's Silver Ring from the strongbox before speaking to Brynjolf to initiate the quest, the ring may disappear from the strongbox without appearing in your inventory. But if you then return to the strongbox during the distraction Brynjolf makes, both the door concealing the box and the box itself will still be unlocked, and the ring will again be in the box, allowing you to steal it once more and proceed with the quest. **?**

## Quest Stages

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Plant Madesi's Ring |

| 35 |  | *(reverse pickpocket failed)* *Objective 30:* Speak to Brynjolf |
| 40 |  | *(player took too long/left area)* *Objective 30:* Speak to Brynjolf |
| 200 | ☑ | Brynjolf's scheme in Riften has ended and the promise of more coin has been made. This appears to be the beginning of profitable friendship. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - TG00MaulHandler: 200.
  - TG00: 0, 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG00 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG00`.

# Skyrim:A Cornered Rat

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").** |

|  |  |

| Quest Giver: | [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), [The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") |

| Suggested Level: | 8 |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") | | → Next | [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") | | |

Esbern in his room in the Warrens

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").
2. Talk to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") or talk to [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") in [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb").
3. Search the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") for [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern")'s hideout.
4. Find Esbern in the Ratway Warrens.
5. Talk to Esbern.
6. Bring Esbern back to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") at [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").

### Finding the Rat

After infiltrating the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"), return to [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") and inform [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") of what you learned from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") records. Delphine is surprised to know her old colleague and fellow [Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"), [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern"), is reportedly still alive. She tasks you with finding the archivist from his hiding place in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Due to the clandestine nature of the Blades, Delphine gives you a secret phrase to deliver to Esbern to secure his trust when you locate him.
Depending on your standing with the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), the journal will direct you to talk to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"), or search the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") for Esbern.
If you are directed to find Brynjolf, you may speak to him, [Dirge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dirge "Skyrim:Dirge"), or [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man") inside [the Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). All three have an option to [persuade](/wiki/Skyrim:Persuade "Skyrim:Persuade") or bribe them for information on Esbern's location.

**Brynjolf**

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Let me find him first. Dragons are bad for business. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Aye, you've got a point there. **Failed**: Passing on a golden opportunity is worse. | | | | **Passed**: Locate Esbern **Failed**: Nothing |

**Vekel the Man**

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I need to talk to him. I'm a friend. His life's in danger. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Maybe I'm just getting soft in my old age, but I actually believe you. **Failed**: That's a touching story. Now get outta my face. | | | | **Passed**: Locate Esbern **Failed**: Nothing |
| Maybe this will help your memory. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Well... when you put it that way, I think I do know the old guy you're talking about. **Failed**: Big talk for someone with a light purse. | | | | **Passed**: Locate Esbern **Failed**: Nothing |

**Dirge**

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I need to talk to him. I'm a friend. His life's in danger. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: A friend, huh? Well... then it's probably okay if I tell you. **Failed**: I guess you don't hear too well. I never heard of this "friend" of yours. | | | | **Passed**: Locate Esbern **Failed**: Nothing |
| Maybe this will help your memory. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: You know what? I think I do know the guy you're talking about. **Failed**: Maybe it would. If you had it. | | | | **Passed**: Locate Esbern **Failed**: Nothing |
| I can break some of your bones if that's what it's going to take... **(Brawl)** | **Passed**: Easy there. I don't want that kind of trouble. Guy ain't worth it.  **Brawl**: Yeah. That's what it's going to take.  - **Victory**: You're tougher than you look. You got me, fair and square.   - **Now where's Esbern?**   - He lives somewhere in the Ratway Warrens. Must be crazy or desperate to live down there. Maybe both. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | | | | **Passed**: Locate Esbern **Failed**: Brawl |

If you have already joined the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), the Ratway is accessible and you can locate Esbern directly. Speaking with [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava"), the Riften innkeeper, also advances the quest.

### The Ratway

The Ratway and the Ratway Vaults beneath Riften are inhabited by a number of [lowlifes](/wiki/Skyrim:Lowlife "Skyrim:Lowlife"), [vagrants](/wiki/Skyrim:Vagrant "Skyrim:Vagrant"), and three or four Thalmor warriors searching for Esbern. When you reach the door to Esbern's room in the Ratway Warrens, he is cautious of Thalmor agents and initially refuses you entry. You may persuade him by saying Delphine sent you, you can tell him the password Delphine gave you: *"Where were you on the 30th of Frostfall?"*, or you may explain that you are the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin").

### The Dragon's Return

Once Esbern lets you in, he shares his dire predictions about the world: [Alduin the World-Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin")'s return has apocalyptic implications, and Esbern's warnings of this threat have been ignored. He makes it clear that there was no hope until you arrived and that he believed the world was going to end. He agrees to follow you to Delphine's base in Riverwood.

Before leaving, Esbern will quickly search his room for any sensitive information the Thalmor might find. He will also gather some supplies from the chest at the foot of his bed and then be ready to leave. The quest ends here, and the next quest, [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall"), begins.

## Notes

- If any follower is hired before or during the quest, they will not be forced to return to their original location when [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") joins as a second follower.
- If he survives [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), [Gissur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gissur "Skyrim:Gissur") will be seated at a table in [the Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") when you get Esbern's whereabouts from [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man"). After you end conversation with Vekel, Gissur will get up from the table and leave the Flagon. If you are a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), Vekel will suddenly say *"That one, right there, walking out the door! He was one of them asking about that old man you were looking for."* If confronted, Gissur will only rebuff your attempts at conversation, but the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Gissur%27s_Note "Skyrim:Gissur's Note") he carries reveals his true intentions. He can be attacked and killed with no repercussions, and other Thieves Guild members will join the fight on your side if you are a guild member, which may make your escape with Esbern easier. If you choose to follow Gissur to his assigned contact instead of killing him, he will head into the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"). He meets up with two [Thalmor soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Soldier "Skyrim:Thalmor Soldier") and a [Thalmor wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Wizard "Skyrim:Thalmor Wizard") and informs them about you:

:   :   **Gissur**: *"He's/She's in the Flagon right now. Get ready."*
    :   **Thalmor Wizard**: *"You're sure?"*
    :   **Gissur**: *"Of course I'm sure! He/She was asking about Esbern."*
    :   **Thalmor Wizard**: *"Doesn't matter. We'll kill them either way."*

:   At this point they'll all make their way back to the Flagon and accost Vekel (or [Dirge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dirge "Skyrim:Dirge"), if Vekel's dead), demanding to know where you are:

:   :   **Thalmor Wizard**: *"Where is he? The one who was asking about the fugitive hiding in the Ratway?"*
    :   **Vekel**: *"You're in the wrong place to be asking those kind of questions, pal."*
    :   (The Thalmor soldiers draw their weapons.)
    :   **Thalmor Wizard**: *"No. Not yet."*
    :   (The Thalmor soldiers sheathe their weapons.)
    :   **Vekel**: *"You'd better clear out before someone gets hurt."*
    :   **Thalmor Wizard**: *"Your lack of cooperation has been noted. We'll be back if we require further information. You won't get a second chance."*
    :   **Vekel**: *"The answer ain't gonna be any different the next time. Arrogant elven bastard."*

:   The Thalmor will then leave the Ragged Flagon and go back into the Ratway to wait for you, while Gissur will return to his seat in the Flagon. They will be hostile on sight, so you will only hear the above conversations if you remain hidden throughout.

- If [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement") has been started, Brynjolf cannot be talked to.
- It is possible to proceed directly to Esbern without returning to Delphine first. Esbern will unlock his door if you tell him you are Dragonborn.

## Bugs

- The quest may fail to start after completing [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), and even trying manually start or end it with the console will not work.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  -  You may have to skip forward to the start of the next quest, [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall"), by using the console and typing in `setstage MQ203 5`, which will allow you to continue.
  -  Use console command `setstage MQ202 (stage #)` to force Esbern to open the door and talk again. Stage 160 makes Esbern open the door, if bugged. Stage 170 makes Esbern talk again, if bugged. Another easier way to avoid bugs is to type in `CompleteQuest MQ202`, which would work for any quest value.
- If following Gissur, the Thalmor may never return to the Ragged Flagon or they may be hostile when you get there, causing the second dialogue to be skipped.
- If you have already become a member of the Thieves Guild, Gissur will attempt to get to his Thalmor contact through the Ragged Flagon - Cistern, through the Crypt Secret Entrance (will not get stuck unless you actively follow him through this roundabout path), and back into the Ratway via the river entrance, resulting in an extremely delayed arrival to his contact. The Thalmor and Gissur will then follow the same path in reverse; all the way through the Crypt, Cistern, and back into the Flagon.

## Quest Stages

| A Cornered Rat (MQ202) | | |

| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | The Thalmor are just as puzzled as we are about why dragons are returning. I learned that they are looking for a Blade named Esbern, who Delphine says is an expert on ancient dragon lore. We need to find him before the Thalmor do. *Objective 10:* Talk to Brynjolf *(if no later stage was done and [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business") wasn't started)* |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Search the Ratway for Esbern's hideout |
| 50 |  | The Thalmor are just as puzzled as we are about why dragons are returning. I learned that they are looking for a Blade named Esbern, who is supposed to be an expert on ancient dragon lore. I've learned that he's hiding out in the Ratway Warrens in Riften. *Objective 30:* Find Esbern in the Ratway Warrens |
| 150 |  | The Thalmor are just as puzzled as we are about why dragons are returning. I learned that they are looking for a Blade named Esbern, who is supposed to be an expert on ancient dragon lore. I found Esbern hiding in the Ratway in Riften, and convinced him to let me in to explain myself. *Objective 40:* Talk to Esbern |
| 180 | ☑ | The Thalmor are just as puzzled as we are about why dragons are returning. I learned that they are looking for a Blade named Esbern, who is supposed to be an expert on ancient dragon lore. I found Esbern hiding in the Ratway in Riften, and convinced him to let me in to explain myself. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 5, 55, 56, 60, 65, 70, 100, 130, 140, 145, 160, 170, 175, 200, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ202 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ202`.

# Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Daedric.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Daedric.png) | **Help [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") reunite with his [master](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") |
| Location(s): | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame"), [Rimerock Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Rimerock_Burrow "Skyrim:Rimerock Burrow") |
| Reward: | [The Rueful Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rueful_Axe "Skyrim:The Rueful Axe") or  [The Masque of Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Skyrim:Masque_of_Clavicus_Vile "Skyrim:Masque of Clavicus Vile") |
| ID: | DA03 |
| Required Level: | 10 |

The Shrine of Clavicus Vile

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").
2. Track down [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas").
3. Travel with Barbas to [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame").
4. Retrieve the [Rueful Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rueful_Axe "Skyrim:The Rueful Axe") for [Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Skyrim:Clavicus_Vile "Skyrim:Clavicus Vile").
5. Give the Rueful Axe to Clavicus Vile *or* kill Barbas.

### Man's Best Friend

A stray dog outside Falkreath

Once you reach the required level, a trip to [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") will net you an encounter with a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard") asking a rather unusual question, namely if you have seen a stray dog running around outside town. Regardless of your answer, he will then point you to the local blacksmith, [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod"), who can be found working his smithy during the day. When approached Lod will only show interest in one specific dog, a 'fine, strong creature that's been wandering near town', that he would like for you to catch for him. You can either accept his request to chase down the dog or pass an always successful [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Impossible_to_Fail "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him to pay you part of the gold up-front for your efforts. In either case, Lod will give you some [fresh meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Fresh_Meat "Skyrim:Food") for bait.

Travel along the road a short distance southwest of town. A dog will approach and enthusiastically address you, saying *"You are exactly what I was looking for"*. He will introduce himself as [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") and will ask for your help. Choose the second dialogue option for a bit of background explanation. Barbas will describe a falling-out that he had with his master, and says that he needs someone who can settle the disagreement. Taunting Barbas will make him reveal his master to be Daedric Prince [Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Skyrim:Clavicus_Vile "Skyrim:Clavicus Vile"), who governs over bargains. You agree to arbitrate this disagreement and Barbas tells you that Vile is probably close to a cult of worshippers living near [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame"). Barbas will then be on his way towards this cavern, and you will have to follow him on a long journey.

Note that traveling with Barbas can be avoided by postponing his request during the second set of dialogue responses; select "You were looking for me?" followed by "I've got things to do". This will make Barbas travel to Haemar's Shame alone. You can then make your way to the shrine when you are ready. If you haven't discovered Haemar's Shame, you can travel to [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") and head east for a relatively uneventful trip. If you choose this option, you can [skip the next section](#Haemar.27s_Shame).

### A Long Journey

Haemar's Shame is located a long way from [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), at the foot of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"), straight east from the ruined town of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). Following Barbas can be difficult as Barbas tends to get lost on occasion, so keep an eye on the map marker. The first distraction comes when you and Barbas face an unmarked bridge guarded by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), just west of Falkreath. Barbas cannot be killed because he is invulnerable, so just fight the opposition and keep an eye on the dog, who may wander off. Follow Barbas past [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch") and up the mountain towards Helgen. The trip goes through the destroyed town, now occupied by bandits, so help Barbas fight them. When all is said and done, Barbas will open the eastern gate himself and continue towards the Throat of the World. When you finally reach Haemar's Shame, Barbas will enter right away so follow him inside.

### Haemar's Shame

Clavicus Vile obviously suffered the same fate as many other daedric princes, and his shrine is now hidden away in a damp tomb. His worshipers consist of leveled [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") who will protect the shrine with their lives. The first room offers an enemy guarding the wooden structure and a chest. Barbas will run ahead, so you will likely be on your own. Take the eastern tunnel and beware of the [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Traps") trap ahead. The next chamber contains a campfire and a charred [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures#Skeever "Skyrim:Creatures") guarded by two vampires. Dispose of them and investigate the wooden structure for an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and another chest. Take the only available tunnel to a chamber in two levels, with several enemies to fight. Take a detour to the southern chamber for some loot, and examine the table on your way down for the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[Response to Bero's Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Response_to_Bero%27s_Speech "Skyrim:Response to Bero's Speech")*, then pick the northern tunnel and exit Haemar's Cavern.

Barbas curing vampirism!

In the next zone, Haemar's Shame, head through the tunnel and kill the residing [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures#Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Creatures"). An [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") can be found in the next room, along with a soul gem and common books. Head downstream and fight the opposition until you reach the Shrine of [Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Skyrim:Clavicus_Vile "Skyrim:Clavicus Vile"), guarded by a boss-leveled vampire. Evident by his barking, Barbas will already be there, busy fighting the boss. After the fight, Barbas will sit in front of the statue with nothing to say but the occasional *"Woof"*. Head up to the statue, activate it, and ask Clavicus Vile if you can make a request. He'll agree to hear it by saying,

:   :   Clavicus Vile: *"By all means, let's hear it. It's the least I could do, since you already helped me grant one final wish for my last worshipers... They were suffering so from vampirism, and begged me for a cure. Then you came and ended their misery! I couldn't have planned it better myself. So, what's your heart's desire? What kind of deal can we strike?"*

If you mention Barbas, he will deny the request but then equivocate.

:   :   Clavicus Vile:*"Ugh. That insufferable pup? Forget it. Request denied. No deal. I'm glad to be rid of him. Even if it does mean I'm stuck in this pitiful shrine, in the back end of... nowhere. Well... perhaps there is a way he could earn his place back at my side. Maybe. But no promises."*

You can also ask for an end to the Civil War in Skyrim to which Clavicus will reply, *"Oh, if I had my full power, granting that would be trivial. I'd simply snap my fingers, and everyone in Skyrim would die. War resolved."*

You can also ask for power to which Clavicus will reply, *"Really? Power? You're a dragonborn; you already have more power than most people who aren't immense fire-breathing monsters."* or *"Really? Power? Haven't you already killed enough of your foes using the more mundane means at your disposal? Swords, magic, etc.? How...uninspired."*, depending on whether or not you have completed [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising").

Clavicus will conclude the last two options with: *"As much as I hate to say it, you're almost as powerful as I am right now. But that's just because half of my power resides in that mutt, Barbas. Come to think of it, I know of a win-win situation for both of us."*

Whatever option you pick, Clavicus is only interested in one thing, the [Rueful Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rueful_Axe "Skyrim:The Rueful Axe"), an axe powerful enough for Clavicus to have *"quite a bit of fun"*. Clavicus will reveal that the axe is located in [Rimerock Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Rimerock_Burrow "Skyrim:Rimerock Burrow") and will ask you to take Barbas with you.

Talking to Barbas will provide a bit of background information on the axe:

:   :   Barbas: *"One of Clavicus's little jests. A wizard named [Sebastian Lort](/wiki/Skyrim:Sebastian_Lort "Skyrim:Sebastian Lort") had a daughter who worshiped Hircine. When the daughter became a werewolf it drove Sebastian over the edge. He couldn't stand to see his little girl take on such a bestial form. The wizard wished for the ability to end his daughter's curse. Clavicus gave him an axe."*

### Rimerock Burrow

Barbas throws himself at Sebastian Lort

Rimerock Burrow is located on the hillside in the northwest corner of the map and can be tricky to find, especially if you approach it from the wrong angle. Take the road leading south from [Lost Echo Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Echo_Cave "Skyrim:Lost Echo Cave") and follow it as it twists and turns. At the crossroads, take the snowy path leading northwest and you will get straight to the entrance. You can also take the ferry from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") to [Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty"), then travel southeast and scale the cliff side until you reach the entrance.

Once inside, you will encounter a hostile [leveled atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), presumably created by [Sebastian Lort](/wiki/Skyrim:Sebastian_Lort "Skyrim:Sebastian Lort") as an extra guardian. Sebastian himself can be found in the next room, equally hostile and will not hesitate to use his [conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spells. After the battle, claim the [Rueful Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rueful_Axe "Skyrim:The Rueful Axe") from the table and examine the room for a bit of loot, an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") and the Conjuration [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Hearth Fire, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")* on Sebastian's nightstand in the following room. It is now time to return to Clavicus Vile in Haemar's Shame.

### Put Him Out of Our Misery!

Barbas at Clavicus Vile's statue

Back at Haemar's Shame, the map marker will point towards the cavern entrance, which will force you to travel through the entire cave system once again. To circumvent this, head west up the road until the path bends. A pine is growing on the left, against the mountain wall; the back entrance is behind this tree below the top of the tree. Reaching the back entrance is fairly easy. If you reach the first piled-up set of rocks on the left, you've gone too far. Note that this only works if you previously opened the spike gate by pulling the chain behind Clavicus Vile's statue. Otherwise, the gate will be closed and you will not be able to access the room. Inside the cavern, Barbas will once again sit in front of his master. When approached, Clavicus Vile has one final prank to play and will give you a choice: you can keep the Rueful Axe if you use it to kill Barbas. The dog will understandably jump up and try to tell you that it is not the only option available. Speak to Barbas and Clavicus Vile for further elaboration and make a decision. Kill Barbas and keep the Rueful Axe, or hand the axe to Clavicus Vile and receive his true daedric artifact, namely the [Masque of Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Skyrim:Masque_of_Clavicus_Vile "Skyrim:Masque of Clavicus Vile"). Note that both items are unique, but only the Masque of Clavicus Vile counts towards the [Oblivion Walker](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") achievement, so it is recommended to keep Barbas alive. Regardless of your choice, Barbas and Clavicus Vile will be reunited and you will receive your reward. Finally, return to [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod") in Falkreath for a small amount of gold and his gratitude.

## Notes

- You may choose not to complete this quest in order to instead keep Barbas as an invincible follower.
- Alternatively, you can complete the quest without ever traveling with Barbas. To do this, don't follow him to Haemar's Shame but let him get there on his own. After accepting the task from Vile, tell Barbas to stop following you.
- If you go through Haemar's Shame without Barbas following you, he will have teleported in, and will already be waiting in front of the Shrine of Clavicus Vile by the time you get there.
- You can receive the gold reward from Lod after speaking with Barbas for the first time, rather than waiting until the quest is finished.
- Prior to the quest, a leveled conjurer will inhabit [Rimerock Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Rimerock_Burrow "Skyrim:Rimerock Burrow"). When the quest is started, that conjurer will be renamed Sebastian Lort.
- With the appropriate dialogue choices, Clavicus Vile will begrudgingly admit that without Barbas, he would be no more powerful than the Dragonborn, adding that giving you more power would be redundant.
- If you spare Barbas, Clavicus will comment on the request you made with him.
  - If your request was to reunite him with Barbas, Clavicus's response will be *"It's a shame you wished for something so dull as me taking back the mutt. Quite the lack of imagination on your part. A lack of ambition like that really ought to be punished. Perhaps by turning you into a worm, or a few decades of..."*
  - If your request was to end the war, Clavicus's response will be *"Now, as for your wish... An end to the war, was it? I'll make sure this war ends, all right. Just as soon as dragons swarm across Skyrim and wipe out all of you puny..."*
  - If your request was for power, Clavicus's response will be *"Now, as for your wish... Power, was it? You can be part of a tremendous power - all you have to do is let your soul be absorbed by this axe. I never said it would be your power..."*
    - Regardless of your request, Clavicus gives you the Masque and says *"Oh, fine. Have my boon and be done with it. Got more interesting deals to make, anyway."*
- It is possible to obtain both artifacts. Near the boss chest above the shrine, activate the shrine and begin the ending dialogue. When it comes time to choose between the items, choose to forfeit the Axe and get the Masque. Exit dialogue immediately and race behind you to the cave exit. It is highly recommended that [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") be used to increase your odds of success. Once outside, quickly fast travel to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and enter [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome"), placing the Axe on a weapon rack. You'll soon receive the Masque and the quest will be completed, and the Rueful Axe will also be available.
- If you and Barbas encounter any [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilant of Stendarr"), they will attack him on sight. Unfortunately, since Barbas is invulnerable, they will perish.
- The quest is reminiscent of Oblivion’s [Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Oblivion:Clavicus_Vile "Oblivion:Clavicus Vile") Daedric Quest, during which you can get either a powerful weapon or his visage as a reward.

## Bugs

- Returning to Haemar's Shame after finishing the quest can cause the game to crash.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- If Lod is dead, guards may still direct you to speak with him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- If you decide not to kill Barbas, and talk to him before he gets turned into stone, the whole statue of Clavicus Vile will disappear and Barbas will remain in the room forever. He will no longer follow you or respond to you in any way but remains stuck in your party restricting your ability to recruit any dog companions thereafter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- If you spare Barbas, the prompt to activate the shrine may still be present after the quest is finished, though activating it will do nothing. **?**
- Telling Barbas to wait inside Rimerock Barrow may cause him to disappear the moment you take the axe. If you choose to kill Barbas, it is possible to follow the map marker and find him drifting around in the wilderness. Use the axe to kill him and the quest will proceed as normal. **?**
- If you tell Barbas to stop following you and then fast travel, he may disappear and not be where he was supposed to be when you return. This will occur even if you simply tell him to stay while at a landmark then immediately open the map and fast travel to that landmark.
  - The best way to avoid this is to simply make sure Barbas is following you before you fast travel anywhere.
- If you don't travel to Haemar's Shame with Barbas, then when you get there, he will be in the final room where Clavicus is. Sometimes, he and all of the vampires in the cell will be behind the exit gate, fighting. If the fighting causes them to go past the trigger point where the game moves you outside, you'll have to use projectiles to kill the vampires.
- Persuading Lod to pay you up front does not grant experience to Speech, nor does it increase the statistics counter for successful persuasions.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA03`.

# Skyrim:A Dying Wish

A strange altar

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Altar "Skyrim:Mysterious Altar") in [Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink").
2. Travel to the [Roadside Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Roadside_Ruins "Skyrim:Roadside Ruins").
3. Choose a cup (Fortune, Power, Nothing).
4. If you chose Fortune, find a bed and sleep. This quest will end and [Fortunate Son](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortunate_Son "Skyrim:Fortunate Son") will begin.
   If you chose Power, find a bed and sleep. This quest will end and [The Pit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pit_(quest) "Skyrim:The Pit (quest)") will begin.
   If you chose Nothing, go back to Falkreath. The quest will continue.
5. Locate a Ferryman to take you to Giant's Tooth.
6. Recover the Iron Wood Fruit.
7. Return to where you left from.
8. Cook soup from Ironwood Fruit (Ironwood Fruit, Charred Skeever Hide, Salt Pile).
9. Travel to Temple of Kynareth in Whiterun.
10. Give soup to priestess.
11. Wait a day to speak with Rulnik.

### The Choice

Mysterious Altar note

In [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), go to the [Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink") and into the owner's room where you will find a note entitled *[Mysterious Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Altar "Skyrim:Mysterious Altar")*. Read it to start the quest. Once read, you will be sent on to the [Roadside Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Roadside_Ruins "Skyrim:Roadside Ruins"). There, you will find several dead bandits and a [Spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") waiting for you. Deal with the Spriggan and in the center of the ruins there is a leveled chest and the strange altar with three cups on it.

- If you chose Fortune, find a bed and sleep. This quest will end and [Fortunate Son](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortunate_Son "Skyrim:Fortunate Son") will begin.

- If you chose Power, this quest will end and [The Pit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pit_(quest) "Skyrim:The Pit (quest)") will begin.

- If you choose Nothing, this quest will continue and you need to head back to town.

### Path of Nothing

Find an Ironwood tree

Upon returning to civilization, you will be approached by a courier with a *[Note from the Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_from_the_Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Note from the Temple of Kynareth")*. The note instructs you to find a ferryman to take you to the location of the Iron Wood Tree to get the fruit, [Giant's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Giant's Tooth"). Only [Harlaug](/wiki/Skyrim:Harlaug "Skyrim:Harlaug") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") will agree to bring you.

On arrival, there is a giant camp with two giants. You can sneak by them to the path behind the camp or kill them. Once done with the giants, follow the path to the [Iron Tusk Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Tusk_Cave "Skyrim:Iron Tusk Cave"). Find the Iron Wood tree and harvest the fruit from it. You will then be attacked by several Spriggans. Defeat them and head back the way you came. Three [Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") will spawn in the giant camp when you emerge and you will need to fight your way back to the boat to return to Dawnstar.

Arriving back at Dawnstar, you will need to prepare a bowl of [Ironwood Soup](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironwood_Soup "Skyrim:Ironwood Soup") using three ingredients: the ironwood fruit, [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). The nearest cooking station is in [Silus Vesuius's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius%27s_House "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius's House"). You will already have been given a charred skeever hide when you received the letter from the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), so all you need to find is some salt. Look in the Fish Barrels outside the cave on Giant's Tooth, and you should find some. Once you have the soup, head for [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and the Temple of Kynareth.

Acolyte Aldren and Rulnik

At the temple, give the soup to [Acolyte Aldren](/wiki/Skyrim:Acolyte_Aldren "Skyrim:Acolyte Aldren") who sent you the note. If you demand payment, you receive 75 gold. She will give the soup to Rulnik and you will be told to wait a full day before checking in on him. Wait a day and come back. Talk to Rulnik and you will receive your rewards: [Rulnik's Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Rulnik%27s_Dagger "Skyrim:Rulnik's Dagger"), the [Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup_(item) "Skyrim:Bittercup (item)"), and a note titled *[On the Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:On_the_Bittercup "Skyrim:On the Bittercup")*. The Bittercup acts as a [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and will raise your highest [attribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Attributes "Skyrim:Attributes") by 20 points at the cost of 20 points from your lowest. For choosing the path of nothing, you will also gain Rulnik as a follower. He is a powerful mage with a level cap of 75, and he can also be appointed as a [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward"). Rulnik's Dagger does the same damage as an Elven dagger, but weighs slightly less. It can be improved with a quicksilver ingot.

## Notes

- After quest completion, you can return to Giant's Tooth island via the same ferryman and go back in the Iron Tusk Cave where the fruit will respawn. If [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") is active, you'll be able to make Hot Ironwood Soup as well. No matter which path is chosen, Ironwood Fruit will become available from [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders").

I used it to craft a bowl of Ironwood soup and delivered it to a priestess. I should check on the man at the temple to see if it has taken effect. *Objective 170:* Check on Rulnik |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccKRTSSE001_zQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccKRTSSE001_zQuest`.

# Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)

## Overview

This article is about the Imperial version of this mission. For the Stormcloak version, see [A False Front (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Imperial Legion.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Imperial_Legion.png) | **Find and deliver some forged [documents](/wiki/Skyrim:StormCloak_Documents "Skyrim:StormCloak Documents") to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") |
| Location(s): | [Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp"), [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"), [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"), [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") |
| Reward: | 5 gold and [Leveled gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | CWMission03 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)") | **Concurrent** [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")—Umbrella quest | **Next →** [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)") | | |

.jpg)

A Stormcloak courier leaving an inn

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp").
2. Find a [Stormcloak courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Courier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Courier") and take his [documents](/wiki/Skyrim:StormCloak_Documents "Skyrim:StormCloak Documents").
3. Take the documents back to Legate Rikke.
4. Take the modified documents to [Frorkmar Banner-Torn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frorkmar_Banner-Torn "Skyrim:Frorkmar Banner-Torn") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").
5. Return to Legate Rikke.

### The Pale

*"One way or another, get me those documents."*

After successfully defending [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") on behalf of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), the umbrella quest [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") will start, as it is high time to conquer all remaining holds currently controlled by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") and once and for all rid Skyrim of [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"). Unless you used it for negotiations during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), your very first target will be to claim [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") to the north. As [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") puts it: *"You'd be wasted as a regular soldier. I have special plans for you. You'll be of greater use to me with greater flexibility. Make your way to our hidden military camp in the Pale. Rikke will have important tasks for you, and will need you when we reclaim the capital."*

When Tullius asks you to [regain the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Regain_the_Pale "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), your commander-in-chief [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") will relocate to the snowy [Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp") east of hold capital [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). Rikke will be located in the easternmost tent, busy studying a huge regional map of Skyrim. When you report for duty she will let you in on her plan to conquer the Pale: *"I need you to deliver some false orders to the Stormcloak commander in Dawnstar. But first we need to get our hands on some rebel orders to make the forgeries."* She will then explain that a [Stormcloak courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Courier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Courier") will travel back and forth between [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") in Ulfric's home city [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), and [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"), a remote inn between Dawnstar and Windhelm. She will then task you: *"See if you can't 'convince' one of those innkeepers to help you. One way or another, get me those documents. But don't do anything rash if you go to Windhelm."* Obviously, Rikke recommends the Nightgate Inn due to its remote location, but leaves the decision and strategy to you.

### The Stormcloak Courier

Your first objective is to find the busy courier. He is quite hard to corner in the wilderness, as he will run back and forth between Candlehearth and Nightgate, and your map markers will only point to the taverns, making it hard to know where the courier is. You will have to either meet him by accident, or ask the innkeepers for his whereabouts. Some useful knowledge is displayed below:

- The courier will never stay long at the inns, and will leave soon after your arrival.
- The only settlement the courier passes through is [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill"). It is possible to wait for the courier there and get the more accurate map marker.
- The courier owns the second room on the left inside both inns, and will reside there if he is present.
- The courier may be killed by wild animals or [Viinturuth](/wiki/Skyrim:Viinturuth "Skyrim:Viinturuth") while traveling, so if he fails to show up after a while, you'll probably have to go out and look for him yourself.

As an alternative to meeting the courier and getting the map marker by chance, you can follow Rikke's advice and ask the innkeepers. Both the innkeeper of Candlehearth Hall, [Elda Early-Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Elda_Early-Dawn "Skyrim:Elda Early-Dawn"), and Nightgate's [Hadring](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadring "Skyrim:Hadring") have the same dialogue and they will have to be persuaded, bribed, or intimidated as they will both say: *"I tend to keep my patrons' privacy."* Note that you will need a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill level of 50 or above to successfully persuade the innkeepers, and that you will always get your answer when intimidating, as it is not possible to fail:

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *"His life is in danger."*  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"It is? Well that's different."*  **Failed**: *"Yeah, sure it is. You don't fool me."* | **Passed**: Map marker  **Failed**: Nothing |
| *"Maybe some gold will help?"*  **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: *"Well, if you insist..."*  **Failed**: *"Seems your purse is lighter than you thought."* | **Passed**: Map marker  **Failed**: Nothing |
| *"I don't have time for this... I can get rough with you if I have to."*  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: *"Now, now! That won't be necessary."* | **Passed**: Map marker |
| *"Never mind."* | *"Hmph."* | Nothing |

When you have successfully finished the persuasion, both innkeepers will now say: *"He's in the inn. Look around. I'm sure you'll find him."*, if the courier is present, or *"He was here, but he left. If you leave now, you can probably catch him. Or, you can just wait here. He'll be back soon enough."*

### Retrieve the Intelligence

_03.jpg)

The courier attacks.

Regardless of your method of locating the courier, the map marker will now point directly to him. Regardless of what you say, or what uniform you are wearing, the Stormcloak courier will not give up the [documents](/wiki/Skyrim:StormCloak_Documents "Skyrim:StormCloak Documents") without a fight, with the inevitable result. When you approach the courier, you will have no options but to say: *"I'm not here to talk. I'm here for those documents."*, and the courier will respond: *"Is that so?"* or *"We'll see about that."* The courier will then proceed to attack, leading to his inevitable death. There is only one way to avoid bloodshed:

- Pickpocket the documents from the courier. This is easily done when the courier relaxes in his room at Candlehearth Hall, as no witnesses will be present.

Killing the courier will always count as murder, even when done with no witnesses around (see Bugs section). However, there are a few ways to make the courier die:

- When he leaves an inn, follow him into the wilderness and wait for the wildlife to kill him.
- Insult him and make him follow you into the wilderness and locate some wildlife that can finish him off.

Lastly, you can kill him yourself. The goal is to do it when no witnesses are around to avoid a bounty. The two methods above will always lead him into seclusion in the wilderness and work perfectly. Additionally, the courier can be stealthily killed inside his room at Candlehearth, especially if he decided to sleep. It goes without saying that Nightgate is the safest spot to achieve your goal, as Windhelm guards will be all over you if you cause a racket in their city. When the courier is dead, claim the documents from the body and head back to Legate Rikke in the camp.

### The Commander of Dawnstar

_02.jpg)

[Frorkmar Banner-Torn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frorkmar_Banner-Torn "Skyrim:Frorkmar Banner-Torn")

When you return to Legate Rikke and hand her the documents, she will immediately start forging the documents, saying: *"Very good... Let's see what you have here. Interesting... They know more of our plans than I expected... It would seem Fort Dunstad is in need of reinforcements... We'll make sure they won't be getting those... One moment while I 'correct' some of these documents... That should do it. Make sure those forged documents get to the Stormcloak commander in Dawnstar. It'll throw him off our trail, allowing us to maneuver more freely."*

When you arrive at [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), follow the map marker to [Frorkmar Banner-Torn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frorkmar_Banner-Torn "Skyrim:Frorkmar Banner-Torn"), who will most likely stand near the Skyrim map inside [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"). When you approach him, his dialogue will differ depending on your choice of armor.

If you are wearing anything but [Stormcloak armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Stormcloak_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"), he will get suspicious: *"Is that so? I don't recognize you. Why aren't you wearing your Stormcloak colors?"* You will then have to tell him it is easier to sneak past the enemy without the uniform, and he will admit: *"I suppose it would be. Good thinking."*

He will then continue on, saying the same thing as if you were wearing Stormcloak armor: *"All right. Let's take a look... Ah, good. Looks like the reinforcements for the fort are on the way. And we have some information about enemy troop movements as well. Excellent. It's not easy running messages, what with Imperials scouts crawling all over the place. Well done. Why don't you grab yourself a drink at the Windpeak before heading back?"* He then hands you 5 gold as a small token of his appreciation, and the quest will end.

Back in the Pale Imperial Camp, Rikke will reward you with a [leveled amount of gold](#Reward). Inspired by the false information you gave to Frorkmar, she will brief you on your next mission: [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)").

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 400 |
| 10–19 | 600 |
| 20–29 | 800 |
| 30–39 | 1,000 |
| 40+ | 1,200 |

## Notes

- This quest and [A False Front (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)") are different radiant versions of the same quest.
- If [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") is given to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

## Bugs

- Killing the Stormcloak courier will count as murder, even if he attacks you first. If a nearby NPC witnesses your "murder", you will incur a bounty in the Pale or Eastmarch.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.

# Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)

## Overview
