(Stormcloaks).jpg)

*"Oh no you don't!"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Galmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist").
2. Locate the [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Courier "Skyrim:Imperial Courier") at [Four Shields Tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Shields_Tavern "Skyrim:Four Shields Tavern") or [Frostfruit Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn").
3. Retrieve [Imperial documents](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Documents "Skyrim:Imperial Documents") from him.
4. Return them to Galmar Stone-Fist.
5. Take the forged documents to [Legate Taurinus Duilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Taurinus_Duilis "Skyrim:Legate Taurinus Duilis") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").
6. Return to Galmar Stone-Fist.

### Acquiring the documents

[Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") will tell you that you need to deliver false orders to an Imperial Legate in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") but first you intercept and steal plans from an [Imperial courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Courier "Skyrim:Imperial Courier"). He tells you that [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") and [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") are frequented often by Imperial couriers, and you should look in the inns of those places.

Head to Rorikstead or Dragon Bridge and speak to the innkeeper in the local inn. To find out the courier's location, you must either persuade, bribe, or intimidate the innkeeper.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| His life is in danger. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: It is? Well that's different. **Failed**: Yeah, sure it is. You don't fool me. | | | | **Passed**: Find the courier **Failed**: Nothing |
| Maybe some gold will help? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Well, if you insist... **Failed**: Seems your purse is lighter than you thought. | | | | **Passed**: Find the courier **Failed**: Nothing |
| I don't have time for this... I can get rough with you if I have to. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Now, now! That won't be necessary. | | | | **Passed**: Find the courier |
| Never mind. | Hmph. | | | | Nothing |

.jpg)

*"His life is in danger."*
 *"It is? Well that's different."*

The innkeeper will then tell you that the courier just left, so you could go after them, or you can wait for the courier to come back. It's better to find the courier in the wilderness because you will get a bounty for killing them. The courier may be far from town, so you it might be better to wait for them to come back and then follow them out of the town. Once you find the courier, saying you want the documents will make the courier attack you immediately.You may also pickpocket the documents off of the courier. The courier may also get into a fight with Stormcloaks or wild animals. Stormcloaks and hostile bandits often frequent the courier's route.

### Delivering the documents

Once you have the documents, head back to the Stormcloak camp and give them to Galmar. He will then forge false information and will then tell you to take them to the [Legate](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Taurinus_Duilis "Skyrim:Legate Taurinus Duilis") in Morthal. Head to Morthal and enter the [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall"), the Legate is through the doorway, under the stairs, to the left. Talk to him and give him the documents, if you are not wearing a Legion uniform he will ask about it, but upon explaining yourself he will take the documents and give you five gold. Now report back to Galmar to prepare for [the Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)").

## Notes

- This quest and [A False Front (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)") are different radiant versions of the same quest.
- Since Rorikstead is in Whiterun hold, which has already been conquered by the Stormcloaks, you can simply wait for him to show up there and watch the Stormcloak guards slaughter him.
- When you speak to the courier demanding the documents he will become hostile and attack you, but killing him will still count as a murder. The easiest way to avoid the murder charge is to get a little in front of him on the road and trigger the bandits hostilities at Robber's Gorge. They usually capably dispose of him. Without your character triggering the bandit ambush he usually makes his trips unharmed.
- If you are wanted in Hjaalmarch, you will be unable to complete this quest until your bounty is resolved, as the Imperial Legate will try to arrest you when you speak with him.

## Bugs

- Be careful about entering Frostfruit Inn to confront the courier while he is in there. He will usually be sleeping in the right hand room when you enter, and when he rises will stand up on the wrong side of the bed causing him to clip through the wall and even fall off the map.

:   - To fix this, wait 1 hour in the inn. The courier will then jump to the other side of the bed allowing you to continue with the game as normal.

- Killing the Imperial courier will count as murder, even if he attacks you first. If a nearby NPC witnesses your "murder", you will incur a bounty in Hjaalmarch, Haafingar, or Whiterun Hold.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWMission03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWMission03`.

# Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Develop your farm.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatic after completing [The Unquiet Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Unquiet_Dead "Skyrim:The Unquiet Dead") |
| Location(s): | [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | ccVSVSSE004\_RestoreFarmQuest |
| Added by: | [Farming](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Unquiet Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Unquiet_Dead "Skyrim:The Unquiet Dead") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Unquiet Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Unquiet_Dead "Skyrim:The Unquiet Dead") | | |

Set up a farming operation

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Plant 10 crops. *(Any [plantable food or ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Fertile_Soil "Skyrim:Fertile Soil"))*
2. Recruit a [Personal Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") for your plantation.
3. Recruit [farmhands](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmhand "Skyrim:Farmhand") to help you with the tasks. *You can ask your steward to hire them.*
4. Build an [animal pen](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction").
5. Talk to your steward about purchasing livestock.
6. Wait a few days before the Goldenhills plantation starts to pay off.
7. Talk to your steward to collect the day's income.
8. Collect the products of the harvest in the pantry.

### Farming

Once you have completed [The Unquiet Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Unquiet_Dead "Skyrim:The Unquiet Dead"), [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation") is now yours. You will be given this quest to walk you through the various farming activities needed to get the place up and running.

Your first step will be to plant 10 crops in any of the plots of [Fertile Soil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fertile_Soil "Skyrim:Fertile Soil") around the property. There are plenty of plots on the property, and you can change your selection of crops at a later date if you so choose. Once this is complete, you will be prompted to hire a [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward"). Many potential [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") will be willing to work as your steward if you bring them to the farm. You can also move your [spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Spouse "Skyrim:Spouse") to Goldenhills and ask them to take over as steward instead.

### Stewardship

With your choice of steward in place, the next step will be to hire some manual labor for the farm. You can speak to your steward about this and they will hire two generic [farmhands](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmhand "Skyrim:Farmhand"). Alternatively, if you wish to provide your own hires, you can recruit [Angrenor Once-Honored](/wiki/Skyrim:Angrenor_Once-Honored "Skyrim:Angrenor Once-Honored"), [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin"), [Embry](/wiki/Skyrim:Embry "Skyrim:Embry"), or [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi").

Once you have hired two farmhands, you will be prompted to [construct](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction") an animal pen. This will require you to use the [Farmer's Workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer%27s_Workbench "Skyrim:Farmer's Workbench") near the entrance to the farmhouse. There are several construction options available, but for the animal pens all you will need is three [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") and a set of [nails](/wiki/Skyrim:Nails "Skyrim:Nails"). Build it and you will be prompted to purchase some livestock via your steward. They will arrange for the purchase of [cows](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow"), [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"), and [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") for the farm.

### Harvest

With all this in place, you now have a fully operational farm. You will have to wait a few days for the plantation to begin turning a profit. When your first income is available, you will be prompted to collect payment from your steward. Your farm will continue to generate revenue passively, which you can collect from your steward at your leisure.

The final step to complete this quest will be to investigate the Pantry Cupboard inside the farmhouse, down the stairs. Open it and you will receive the following tutorial message:

:   *Crops, milk, and eggs produced by the farm will be automatically stored in this cupboard.*

Within the cupboard you should find the first few samples of auto-harvested crops. This cupboard will continue to be filled passively over time, depending on what you choose to grow on the farm.

Congratulations, you have completed setting up your farm! There are plenty of other upgrades and activities to do at Goldenhills to develop it into a truly profitable enterprise.

## Notes

- If you hire Narfi, you may still have to kill him later for an early Dark Brotherhood writ. It is possible to hire another farmhand to replace him if this occurs.

## Bugs

- You might not get the dialogue options to make any of your followers a steward after planting the crops.
- Even after hiring a steward, the quest marker might be stuck on stage 10.
- It is possible that the quest will not automatically start after completing The Unquiet Dead.

## Quest Stages

| A Farmer's Life For Me (ccVSVSSE004\_RestoreFarmQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | Now that I've laid the ghosts haunting <Alias=FarmLocation> to rest and claimed it for my own, I should see about getting my new homestead restored to its former glory. First I should get some crops in the ground. *Objective 0:* Plant crops (0/10) |
| 10 |  | I should find a steward to manage the day-to-day operations. Perhaps one of my allies would be willing to take on the job after I show them the place? Or I'm sure my spouse could run the farm, if I make this our home. *Objective 10:* Hire a steward for the plantation |
| 10 |  | I should find a steward to manage the day-to-day operations. Perhaps one of my allies would be willing to take on the job after I show them the place? Or if I were to get married, I could make this place our home and my spouse could run the farm. *Objective 10:* Hire a steward for the plantation |
| 20 |  | Now that I have a steward to manage the farm while I'm away, I should see about hiring some farmhands to tend to the crops and animals. I could either ask around in town to see if anyone is looking for work, or I could get my new steward to handle it. *Objective 20:* Recruit a farmhand to help with labor |
| 30 |  | <Alias=FarmLocation> is well on its way towards being a profitable farm again, now that I've planted crops and hired farmhands to tend to them. Next, I should see about acquiring some livestock. *Objective 30:* Build an animal pen |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Talk to <Alias=Overseer> about purchasing livestock |
| 50 |  | The crops are growing and the livestock are thriving. Soon I'll be able to start collecting the profit from my plantation. I should come back in a few days and speak to <Alias=Overseer> to collect what money has been earned. *Objective 50:* Wait a few days for <Alias=FarmLocation> to start making money |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Talk to <Alias=Overseer> to collect the day's profit |
| 70 |  | With <Alias=FarmLocation> thriving again, the excess crops and animal goods will be harvested by my hired help for my personal use. I should check the pantry inside the farmhouse to see what has been collected. *Objective 70:* Collect the extra harvested produce from the pantry |
| 70 |  | With <Alias=FarmLocation> thriving again, the excess crops and animal goods will be harvested by my hired help for my family's use. I should check the pantry inside the farmhouse to see what has been collected. *Objective 70:* Collect the extra harvested produce from the pantry |
| 500 | ☑ | I've returned <Alias=FarmLocation> to the thriving plantation it once was. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccVSVSSE004_RestoreFarmQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccVSVSSE004_RestoreFarmQuest`.

# Skyrim:A Few Words with You

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). ## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from any of the following six people. The person to whom you must talk is uniquely determined by the quest giver.

| Region | Location | Quest Giver | Target | Dialogue Trigger | Reward |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Argonian Assemblage](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Assemblage "Skyrim:Argonian Assemblage") | [Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes") | [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield") | "Someone giving you trouble?" | Two leveled fortify-skill [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") or three leveled restoration potions |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"), [Braidwood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Braidwood_Inn "Skyrim:Braidwood Inn") | [Iddra](/wiki/Skyrim:Iddra "Skyrim:Iddra") | [Roggi Knot-Beard](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggi_Knot-Beard "Skyrim:Roggi Knot-Beard") | "Who's Roggi?" | One unenchanted leveled weapon and armor |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") | [Octieve San](/wiki/Skyrim:Octieve_San "Skyrim:Octieve San") | [Irnskar Ironhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand") | "You're in debt to Irnskar?" | [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill point |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") | [Omluag](/wiki/Skyrim:Omluag "Skyrim:Omluag") | [Mulush gro-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Mulush_gro-Shugurz "Skyrim:Mulush gro-Shugurz") | "You're having trouble with Mulush?" | Leveled amount of gold |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") | [Carlotta Valentia](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia") | [Mikael](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikael "Skyrim:Mikael") | "Someone giving you trouble?" | Leveled amount of gold |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") | [Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") | [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") | "What's wrong with Ranmir?" | One unenchanted leveled weapon and armor |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to the quest giver.
2. Talk to the NPC the quest giver wishes you to speak with.
3. Persuade, bribe, intimidate, or brawl with the target NPC.
4. Return to the quest giver.

### Carlotta Valentia and Mikael

[Carlotta Valentia](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia") is a food vendor who runs a stall at the [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") market. She gets a lot of attention from men in this city and half of them have proposed to her. However, all that matters is her daughter [Mila](/wiki/Skyrim:Mila_Valentia "Skyrim:Mila Valentia") and no man's going to get between them. The bard [Mikael](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikael "Skyrim:Mikael") keeps going on about her and says he'll *"conquer her as a true Nord conquers any harsh beast."* You can talk to Mikael and help her deal with the trouble.

Mikael can be found at the [Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare"), performing or resting. You may tell him to leave Carlotta Valentia alone. He will tell you *"I'm sorry, but that fiery widow is mine. She just doesn't know it yet."* You can then choose between three options. You must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him.

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| She's not yours. Stop this nonsense. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Maybe you're right. I guess I just didn't want anyone to think I couldn't handle one Nord lass. On my honor, I won't bother Carlotta ever again. **Failed**: What did you just say? All I heard was the sound of jealousy. | **Passed**: Return to Carlotta **Failed**: Nothing |
| Maybe we can come to an understanding. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Bribing me? Well, a bard does need to eat. On my ancestor's honor, I won't trouble sweet Carlotta again. **Failed**: I don't think so. | **Passed**: Return to Carlotta **Failed**: Nothing |
| Leave her alone, or else. **(Brawl)** | **Passed**: Whoa. Hey there. I didn't mean to make you upset. On my honor, Carlotta won't have to worry about me again.  **Brawl**: (Start a brawl)  - **Victory**: You know how to throw a punch, I'll give you that.   - **You leave Carlotta alone, or this gets worse.**   - You win. On my honor, Carlotta won't have to worry about me ever again. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | **Passed**: Return to Carlotta **Failed**: Brawl |
| Fine. Forget I asked. | Already have. | Nothing |

Return to Carlotta and tell her Mikael won't be bothering her anymore. She will be a little surprised: *"Really? You convinced that lute player to stop chasing me?"* Then she will thank you and reward you with some gold.

#### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

### Haran and Ranmir

[Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") runs [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") with her husband [Dagur](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagur "Skyrim:Dagur") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). You can find her working there all day long. As a frequent visitor to the tavern, [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") isn't so welcome. Haran may complain to her husband: *"How long are we going to let Ranmir drink himself into a stupor? When will enough be enough?"* If you talk to her about Ranmir, she will tell you *"Ranmir beg a drink from you, yet? That's gold wasted, friend."* Although she can understand he's had some [troubles](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows") in his life, she can't have him drinking here without at least paying back some of the coin he owes.

Ranmir spends almost all his days drinking right in the tavern, explaining *"Nothing to do here but drink till you forget you got nothing to do."* If you ask him to pay Haran back for his drinks, he will be unhappy: *"Who are you to say what I should do? I'll pay her back when I'm ready."* Then you can choose between three options. You must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him.

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| You owe her gold. Pay it. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: You're right. What would my forefathers think if they knew I wasn't paying my debts? Tell Haran I'll bring her the gold I owe. **Failed**: And I told you I'd pay it when I'm good and ready. | **Passed**: Return to Haran **Failed**: Nothing |
| What if I pay it? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: I won't say no to that. **Failed**: I'm not about to take on debts from some milk drinker I don't know. | **Passed**: Return to Haran **Failed**: Nothing |
| Do it, or things get ugly. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Calm down there, friend. I'll pay! Tell Haran that she'll have her gold.  **Failed**: (Start a brawl)  - **Victory**: What was that? Some kind of foreign move?   - **You ready to pay up now?**   - You got me, fair and square. Tell Haran I'll pay. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | **Passed**: Return to Haran **Failed**: Brawl |
| Fine. Forget I asked. | That's what I thought. | Nothing |

Return to Haran and she will admit *"He's not a bad man, just bad with his coins and his drink."* Then she will give you a weapon and a piece of armor in return.

### Iddra and Roggi Knot-Beard

[Iddra](/wiki/Skyrim:Iddra "Skyrim:Iddra") is the innkeeper of the [Braidwood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Braidwood_Inn "Skyrim:Braidwood Inn") in [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"). She thinks highly of [Roggi Knot-Beard](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggi_Knot-Beard "Skyrim:Roggi Knot-Beard") as a storyteller and comments that he can keep everyone's spirits up. Although he owes Iddra a lot of coin for drinks, she keeps telling him not to worry about it. However, his "stubborn Nord blood" doesn't allow him to do so. She will eventually tell you *"Damn fool doesn't have the coin to pay me back, so he just beats himself up over it, and then he gets thirsty, and it cycles all over again."* If you can talk to Roggi, she'd feel better.

Roggi is a miner and he can be found inside Braidwood Inn or in the mining camp nearby. If you tell him to forget about all the coin he owes, he will get a little angry: *"What do you think I am, a beggar? My family has always paid back every single coin we owed, going back to [Tiber Septim](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim")'s time."* You need to choose between three options and must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him. If you have helped him before by [retrieving his ancestral shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)") from a dungeon, he will agree with you: *"I guess if you're telling me to stop worrying about it, maybe I should just let it go. Thank you, friend."*

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stop being stubborn. Let it go. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: I guess you're right. A Nord shouldn't be so proud to turn down a kind soul's generosity. Tell Iddra I'll be fine. **Failed**: No. I have my pride. | **Passed**: Return to Iddra **Failed**: Nothing |
| What if I pay it? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: A true Nord would settle it himself, but at least this way Iddra gets her coin. Thank you. Tell her I'll be fine. **Failed**: This isn't about me paying Iddra back, this is about me being able to pay her back with my own coin. | **Passed**: Return to Iddra **Failed**: Nothing |
| Do I need to beat some sense into you? **(Brawl)** | **Passed**: What? No. All right. I won't worry about the coin anymore, just stop giving me that look.  **Brawl**: (Start a brawl)  - **Victory**: You throw a mean hook.   - **You ready to listen to reason now?**   - I get your point. Tell Iddra I'm sorry for being so stubborn about the coin. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | **Passed**: Return to Iddra **Failed**: Brawl |
| Fine. Forget I asked. | It's better that way. | Nothing |

Return to Iddra and tell her that Roggi won't be complaining anymore. She will say, *"Roggi pawned a few of his things back when he still had things to pawn."* Then she will reward you with a weapon and armor.

### Octieve San and Irnskar Ironhand

[Octieve San](/wiki/Skyrim:Octieve_San "Skyrim:Octieve San") is an old warrior living in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), frequently found in [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever"). As an elder, he enjoys his current life a lot: *"Being old's not so bad. Daughter keeps me fed, and my working days are done."* If you talk to him, he will tell you something annoying behind his relaxed life: *"Take my advice. Never gamble. Damn [Irnskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand") has me in debt up to the eyes."* Too many drinking games, too many bets, and he is too old to ever raise the coin on his own. You may talk to Irnskar and give this old man a hand.

Find Irnskar and talk to him about forgiving Octieve's debts. He will insist, *"Debts are debts. Either he pays them, or his kind do."* Then you will have three options for him. In order to persuade him, you must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech").

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| He's an old man. Let it go. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Fine. You sound like a priest of Mara, but I get your point. Tell him to forget about the gold. **Failed**: A debt. Is a debt. | **Passed**: Return to Octieve **Failed**: Nothing |
| What if I pay it? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Works for me. Tell Octieve the debt's settled. **Failed**: Don't think so. | **Passed**: Return to Octieve **Failed**: Nothing |
| Lay off the old man. Now. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: All right, all right. Have it your way. Tell Octieve to forget about the debt.  **Failed**: (Start a brawl)  - **Victory**: Backbiter.   - **Final warning. Leave Octieve alone.**   - All right. Tell the old man his debts are settled. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | **Passed**: Return to Octieve **Failed**: Brawl |
| Fine. Forget I asked. | That's what I thought. | Nothing |

Bring the good news to Octieve San and he will give you a one-point boost to your [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill and become a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

### Omluag and Mulush gro-Shugurz

[Omluag](/wiki/Skyrim:Omluag "Skyrim:Omluag") lives in [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") and works at the [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). You may also find him in [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn"), enjoying some free time after a whole day's work. During his work, he will often say, *"Can't talk. [Mulush](/wiki/Skyrim:Mulush_gro-Shugurz "Skyrim:Mulush gro-Shugurz") will beat me if I stop working."* If you are interested in his trouble with Mulush, talk to him and he will tell you, *"He's a damn tyrant. Always being goaded on by the Silver-Bloods to get more work out of us. They pay us next to nothing. We get beaten if we make a mistake, and where are our kind Nord rulers? What are they doing? Typical."* If you are willing to talk to Mulush, he will be a little surprised: *"You're going to try to talk sense into that Orc? I'll believe it when I see it."*

You can find Mulush right near his workers, monitoring their work. If you talk to him, he will realize you're not one of his workers and ask your business here. You can ask him to leave Omluag alone. He will only give you a series of questions: *"What? Are you telling me how to treat my workers? Do you have any idea how much metal the Silver-Blood family wants us to smelt?"* You can then choose between three options to reach your goal. You must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade this smelter overseer.

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| You're working him to death. Lay off. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: All right, all right. You sound like a damn Legion officer, but I get it. I'll give him a break. This better not hurt our quota. **Failed**: I'm in charge of the smelter. Not you. So why don't you lay off? | **Passed**: Return to Omluag **Failed**: Nothing |
| Maybe we can come to an understanding. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: I guess I can spare him a few beatings. Deal. **Failed**: The only thing I understand is you bothering you. | **Passed**: Return to Omluag **Failed**: Nothing |
| Then we do this the hard way. **(Brawl)** | **Passed**: Wait. You win. I'll ease off on the beatings, just leave me alone.  **Brawl**: (Start a brawl)  - **Victory**: Damn outsider. Why couldn't you just mind your own business?   - **Leave Omluag alone. This is my final warning.**   - All right. I'll lay off him. Just leave. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | **Passed**: Return to Omluag **Failed**: Brawl |
| Fine. Forget I asked. | Idiot. | Nothing |

Tell Omluag that you convinced Mulush to ease up a bit. He will be very excited and give his a week's wages to you as your payment. *"I don't believe it. Someone sticking up for us."*

#### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

### Scouts-Many-Marshes and Torbjorn Shatter-Shield

[Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes") is an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") dock worker in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He and his clansmen can be seen working around the Windhelm docks. Although race prejudice is quite common in this city, he wishes the Nords, Argonians and Dunmer here got along better. If you talk to him about his trouble, he will tell you something about their boss, [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield"). He wants everything for nothing and clings to every septim. *"He says an Argonian's labor is only worth a tenth of a 'proper Nord worker.' My people are not slaves!"* They have no chance to negotiate with him themselves, but you may try to talk to Torbjorn for him.

You can find Torbjorn in the city, staying in his house or drinking at [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"). You can ask him to pay the Argonians a fair wage. If you have done him a favor before, by either bringing him an [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Amulet of Arkay") or an alcoholic drink, he will listen to you: *"Well, my friend, if you think those boots needs more coin, I'll make it happen. But I'm doing this for you, not them."* Otherwise, he will refuse without hesitation: *"Those boots aren't worth the septims I do pay them. I'm not giving them coin I could give to good, Nord workers."* Then you may choose between three options to change his mind. You must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him.

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| They'll work harder if you pay them more. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Bold words, but true. Fine, you win. I'll pay the Argonians more coin. **Failed**: They don't work now. Why should I waste more money? | **Passed**: Return to Scouts **Failed**: Nothing |
| What if I invest in their future? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Paying the wages yourself? Well, I won't say no to gold. By my family's honor, this money will go to the Argonian workers. **Failed**: What future? | **Passed**: Return to Scouts **Failed**: Nothing |
| Pay them, or things will get ugly. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Easy. Maybe I was being too harsh on them. By the honor of Clan Shatter-Shield, they will be paid fairly. You have my word.  **Brawl**: (Start a brawl)  - **Victory**: Damn boot-lover.   - **You pay those Argonians fairly, or else.**   - I yield. By the honor of Clan Shatter-Shield, the Argonians will be paid as much as any other worker. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | **Passed**: Return to Scouts **Failed**: Brawl |
| Fine. Forget I asked. | That's what I thought. | Nothing |

Return to Scouts-Many-Marshes with the good news and he will be impressed. For your help, he will then give you either two fortify-skill potions or three restoration potions that he was saving.

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* calls this quest "A Good Talking To".
- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold.
- If you have managed to build a friendly disposition with the targeted NPC to speak with, usually by doing quests given by them, the quest can simply skip the need for you to persuade or intimidate the targeted NPC.

## Bugs

- Either possessing one of these quests in the quest log or having completed one, may potentially stop you from being able to marry [Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes"). If you were intending to marry him, complete his task first, get married and then start the other quests.
- The Two-handed skill point awarded by Octieve may not be given.
- You may still receive Irnskar Ironhand as a target even if he is dead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| A Few Words with You (Favor013) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Talk to <Alias.ShortName=Target> about <Alias.ShortName=Questgiver> |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Tell <Alias.ShortName=Questgiver> that <Alias.ShortName=Target> is taken care of |
| 20 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor013 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor013`.

# Skyrim:A Jarl's Justice

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Kill a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") masquerading as a [Visiting Advisor](/wiki/Skyrim:Visiting_Advisor "Skyrim:Visiting Advisor").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") |
| Location(s): | Radiant |
| Reward: | Leveled enchanted item |
| ID: | DLC1RH07 |
| Difficulty: | Hard |

Visiting Advisor at the White Hall in Dawnstar

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran").
2. Warn the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") threat.
3. Find and take [evidence](/wiki/Skyrim:Orders_(DG) "Skyrim:Orders (DG)") to the jarl.
   - *(Alternate)* Discreetly kill the [Visiting Advisor](/wiki/Skyrim:Visiting_Advisor "Skyrim:Visiting Advisor") and return to Isran.
4. Kill the Visiting Advisor.
5. Report back to Isran.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After speaking with [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran"), you will be sent to inform a random [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") threat within their court. The jarl will note the seriousness of your allegation, and ask for evidence. This can be obtained by pickpocketing the [Visiting Advisor](/wiki/Skyrim:Visiting_Advisor "Skyrim:Visiting Advisor"), who can usually be found in the main court room of the jarl's hall, for his [orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Orders_(DG) "Skyrim:Orders (DG)"). Note that if your pickpocket attempt fails he will attack you, often leading to confrontation with nearby NPCs and likely death. This method is particularly effective when you are a [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of the relevant hold, as you will then be able to tell the guards to disregard your crime.

Return to the jarl with the note and they will grant you leave to kill the vampire with no retaliation from the hold's guards. Note that despite nominally being a vampire, the Adviser is immune to the [Sun Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Fire "Skyrim:Sun Fire") spell [*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:A_Jarl%27s_Justice)*]. Alternatively, you can skip the evidence gathering stage and instead discreetly eliminate the Visiting Advisor through either stealth or using a [Frenzy](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(spell) "Skyrim:Frenzy (spell)") spell while hidden. Once the vampire lies dead, return to Isran.

## Notes

- If the Jarl you were to report to is deposed, including via [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), this quest will automatically be completed.
- It is impossible for the advisor to be at the court of [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") or [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), due to their unique voice types.
- Unlike other [Dawnguard radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Quests#Dawnguard_Quests "Skyrim:Dawnguard Quests"), this one can only occur every twelve days at best.

## Bugs

- Isran will only assign Dawnstar or Riften as target locations for this quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- The advisor is supposed to stay within a certain distance of the jarl, but in locations like Understone Keep and occasionally others, this can leave the advisor inside a locked room or in other unintuitive locations.
  - Save and reload the game, or exit the building and re-enter; the advisor may show up in a different location.
  - Wait until the jarl goes to bed or wakes up; this will typically cause the advisor to follow or, if locked in a room, to teleport close to the jarl. (This may require you to leave and re-enter or save and reload.)
  -  Use the following console commands to move directly to the advisor: `sqv DLC1RH07`. Look for the line that starts with Ref 'Vampire' and note the ID in parentheses at the end of that line. Then use `player.moveto ID` and you should be taken directly to the advisor.
- It is not considered a crime to attack the disguised vampire despite being warned by Isran that it would be if you're caught.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

If I fail to secure <Alias=Jarl>'s permission first, the guards will consider it a murder. *Objective 10:* Warn <Alias=Jarl> about the vampire threat |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Find evidence linked to the vampire |

| 100 |  | *Objective 40:* Destroy the vampire masquerading as a Visiting Advisor  *Objective 100:* Return to <Alias=QuestGiver> |
| 255 | ☑ | I've destroyed the vampire in <Alias=Capital> masquerading as a visiting advisor to <Alias=Jarl>'s court. |
| 300 | ☑ | <Alias=Jarl> is no longer the Jarl of <Alias=Capital> and the vampire no longer poses a threat. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RH07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RH07`.

# Skyrim:A Lovely Letter

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Chezburgar](/wiki/User:Chezburgar "User:Chezburgar"), checked by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Use a forged letter to resolve a love triangle.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven") or [Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal") |
| Location(s): | [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") |
| Reward: | 25 Gold, Faendal or Sven as a follower |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =-1 ([Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal")), =2 ([Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven")) *or* =-1 ([Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven")), =2 ([Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiverwood01 |

Camilla Valerius is at the center of a love triangle.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Learn about the love triangle from the townspeople.
2. Talk to [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven") or [Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal") about the love triangle.
   - *(Optional)* Talk to the other man involved in the love triangle (Sven if you talked to Faendal first or vice versa).
3. Give the letter to [Camilla Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Camilla_Valerius "Skyrim:Camilla Valerius").
4. Return to the man you decided to help to finish the quest.

### The Triangle

When you visit the small town of Riverwood, the local beauty, Camilla Valerius, has sparked the interest of two bachelors in town. The local bard, Sven, and the Wood Elf hunter Faendal, are both vying for Camilla's favor; and will resort to slander and libel to win it.

### What a Tangled Web We Weave

If you approach Sven first, at the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn"), you will come to know of his love for Camilla, and about his suspicions about Faendal's involvement in her life. Sven will then ask you for a favor: deliver a [fake letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven%27s_Fake_Letter_from_Faendal "Skyrim:Sven's Fake Letter from Faendal") supposedly written by Faendal to Camilla, seemingly breaking things off with her due to her being an Imperial, and him a proud Bosmer.
You may also speak to Faendal first. He can be found chopping wood near the lumber mill or wandering the village. Faendal also has feelings for Camilla and a desire to see Sven out of the picture. He asks you to deliver his own [fake letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal%27s_Fake_Letter_from_Sven "Skyrim:Faendal's Fake Letter from Sven") designed to disrupt Sven's wooing by outlining out the household chores he has planned for Camilla.
With either letter, you can go straight to Camilla, or show the supposed letter to the other man, prompting them to hand over their own forged letter for you to deliver.

### When We Practice to Deceive

When you decide who you want to help, either Sven or Faendal, deliver the letter to Camilla.
Camilla is usually at the [Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader"), but at night she can sometimes be found at the Sleeping Giant Inn.
When you talk to Camilla, you have two ways of proceeding. You can lie to her and give her the forged letter as is, or tell her the truth about the ruse. In either case, she will effectively break off her interactions with the loser. Speak with the winner to collect your reward.

## Notes

- It is not possible to complete this quest in a manner that has both Sven and Faendal become available as followers and have their dispositions friendly towards you.
- Despite the events of this quest, Camilla is also a [marriage candidate](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") for you, and can be married once her disposition is increased, such as by completing the quest [The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw"). However, this does not in any way alter the events or dialogue of this quest, and all participants will act as if Camilla is still available. If Camilla relocates to one of your houses, and you helped one man win her over, his AI package will still have him seek her out even at your house.

## Bugs

- If this quest is still running when marrying Camilla, it is still possible to finish it by delivering the letter on behalf of one or the other even though this scene no longer makes sense to allow.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. Marrying Camilla while the quest is still active will now cause it to fail.

## Quest Stages

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 7, 105, 107, 200, 310, 320.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiverwood01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiverwood01`.

# Skyrim:A Matter of Pride

A Matter of Pride

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah") to find a copy of [Eranya's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eranya's Journal")
2. Travel to [Sivdur's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite") and read [Eranya's Notes on Sivdur's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Notes_on_Sivdur%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Eranya's Notes on Sivdur's Tomb")
3. Go to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") and read a copy of [Eranya's Research Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Research_Notes "Skyrim:Eranya's Research Notes")
4. Go to Whiterun to fetch Sivdur's Amulet
5. Go to [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow") to fetch Magrathi's skull
6. Travel to [Sivdur's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite") and enter the warrior's tomb
7. Locate Goldbrand

## Detailed Walkthrough

Body of Eranya

There are two locations to start the quest: the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah") and the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").

At the Sacellum of Boethiah in the fenced-in fighting area, you will find [Eranya](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya "Skyrim:Eranya"), an imperial researcher investigating the legendary [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)"). She isn't very eager to tell you the location of it, on account of being dead, but by reading [her journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eranya's Journal") you will find out the katana rests in [Sivdur's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite").

Go to [Sivdur's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite"), located to the north of Windhelm and you will be attacked by a few [cultists of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah_Cultist "Skyrim:Boethiah Cultist"), one of which will have a [note detailing their ambitions](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist%27s_Note "Skyrim:Cultist's Note"). There is a gate with two pedestals on either side of it. Both pedestals have etched tablets. The left one states:

```
   "I, Sivdur, warrior and defender of dragons, lie in rest here
   My amulet, the symbol of my valor
   Place it here so that I may have proof of my deeds in Sovngarde"
```

While the right one states:

```
   "Forever my nemesis, Magrathi, high priest and slayer of my brother
   His skull, the symbol of his betrayal
   Place it here, away from his kinsman, so that he may never find peace"
```

On a table to the right of the pedestals lie [Eranya's Notes on Sivdur's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Notes_on_Sivdur%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Eranya's Notes on Sivdur's Tomb"), which will tell you that her research notes were left at the Arcanaeum at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").

Go there and you will find [Eranya's Research Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Research_Notes "Skyrim:Eranya's Research Notes") located on the floor to the right of Urag gro-Shub's desk among some other books.

Alternatively, you can go straight to the Arcanaeum at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") (or go there after reading [Eranya's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eranya's Journal")) and read the copy of [Eranya's Research Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Research_Notes "Skyrim:Eranya's Research Notes").

Once you've read Eranya's Research Notes, you will be attacked by two invisible [Boethiah Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah_Cultist "Skyrim:Boethiah Cultist"). Each of them will have a potion of invisibility.

You will then need to find two artifacts to complete the quest: Sivdur's Amulet and Magrathi's Skull. They can be found in any order.

### Acquiring Sivdur's Amulet

Visit Whiterun and convince [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born") to give you Sivdur's amulet:

:   **I heard your dad gave you a very old, special amulet. Is that true?**
:   *"Ahh... yeah."*
:   **I need it. Would you give it to me?**
:   *"Go away."*

| Option | Dialogue | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Hand over the amulet, or you won't like what comes next.**  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: *"Don't hurt me! You win."* | | | |
| **I was going to use it to find a magic sword. Isn't that exciting?**  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"How can I argue with that?"* | | | |
| **Would a few shiny septims change your mind?**  **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: *"For that price? Sure."* | | | |

### Acquiring Magrathi's Skull

Magrathi's Skull is a little bit more complicated than the amulet.

Travel to [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") and enter [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow"). If you have not cleared out the barrow beforehand, to the right of you, behind a gate, will be [a ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius_Gatharian "Skyrim:Wyndelius Gatharian"). That ghost is not related to this quest and you do not have to deal with him, but what self-respecting adventurer would pass up [a chance for fame, riches and a word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Lifting_the_Shroud "Skyrim:Lifting the Shroud")?

Magrathi will be in the claw door chamber, past several traps, a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")* and [the ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius_Gatharian "Skyrim:Wyndelius Gatharian"), and, unlike [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born") will be reticent in giving you what you seek. He is a maskless [Dragon Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") and will be just as powerful as any of the others no matter your level, so make sure you are prepared for the difficult fight ahead. After defeating him make sure to take [his skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Magrathi%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Magrathi's Skull").

### Sivdur's Respite

The two tablets and holders

You will now need to head back to [Sivdur's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite"). Place Sivdur's amulet on the pedestal to the left of the door and Magrathi's skull on the pedestal to the right of the door in order to proceed.

The dungeon has some leveled draugr enemies and loot, but it is all of little note except for Sivdur's Tomb, where you will find [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)") on a pedestal and a chest near the entrance. When you pick up Goldbrand, two Honor Guards of Sivdur will get out of their sarcophagi, so be ready to fight them or run away; killing them is not necessary for the completion of the quest.

Sivdur's honor guards

## Notes

- Reading Eranya's Journal at Sivdur's Respite will initiate the miscellaneous journal entry to visit the College of Winterhold if you have not previously been told to visit the College before.
- It is not possible to fail the speech checks for aquiring Sivdur's Amulet from [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born"). If the player does not have enough gold to bribe him the option to do so will not appear in dialogue.
- If this quest is done concurrently with [investigating Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Lifting_the_Shroud "Skyrim:Lifting the Shroud"), you will be dealing with a Dragon Priest in the first zone on top of the insane mage [Wyndelius Gatharian](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius_Gatharian "Skyrim:Wyndelius Gatharian") before you can even reach the claw door and the Word of Power within.

## Bugs

- It appears that the Boethiah Cultists will respawn in the Arcanaeum whenever the cell resets. From there, they stalk you wherever you go, and they can appear anywhere, including inside player homes. They only follow at walking speed, so having them catch up to you may be fairly infrequent and appear to be arbitrary.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.629.0, fixes this bug.
- Entering Sivdur's Respite before starting the quest may set the quest to Stage 400 and prevent the quest from starting normally. **?**
  - This can be fixed by using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `resetquest ccBGSSSE005_MainQuest` to reset the quest.

# Skyrim:A New Debt

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Help [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") with his debt to [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)") |
| Location(s): | [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | DLC2TT1b |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") | | |

A New Debt

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Be informed of your inherited debt by [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)").
2. Pay the debt or kill Mogrul.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After the completion of the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") you will be made aware of a debt that [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") owed to a money lender by the name of [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)") operating out of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). Now that Drovas is under the protection of [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") and out of Mogrul's reach, Mogrul expects you to make good on Drovas' debt. To help entice you to pay the debt, Mogrul will send his [thugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul%27s_Thug "Skyrim:Mogrul's Thug") after you until the debt is paid.

Mogrul will approach you while you are in Raven Rock:

:   *"It seems you've inherited a situation."*

    :   **Situation? What kind of situation?**
    :   *"Drovas Revli*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *owes me 1000 septims. At least he did until you set him up with that [Telvanni](/wiki/Lore:Telvanni "Lore:Telvanni") wizard. Now he's untouchable. The way I figure it, it's your fault he can't pay me. So I guess I'm going to have to collect it from you."*

You will then be presented with several dialogue options:

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **I'm so sorry! Here, take the money.** | *"See, that wasn't so hard, now was it. Now get outta here."* | Pay 1000 gold |
| **And if I don't pay you?** | *"Nothing for now. But watch your back. I'll be sending collectors to find you. They won't ask so nicely. One way or the other, I'll get my money."* | Nothing |
| **Or I could just kill you now.** | *"Take your best shot, fetcher! But if you draw on me, the guards will put the bounty on your head, not mine."* | Nothing |
| **Please be patient. I'll get you your money.** | *"Patience is for fools. When you are tired of looking over your shoulder, you'll pay me."* | Nothing |
| **How about you take half? (Intimidate)** | **Passed**: *"Uh... yeah. That sounds good. Half. I think that will work."* **Failed**: *"How about I don't. You don't scare me."* | **Passed**: Pay 500 gold **Failed**: Nothing |

If you decide to pay him later:

:   **About that money Drovas owes you...**
:   *"Tired of running? I knew you were weak. Now pay me."*

At this point, you will have the same dialogue options as above.

Mogrul's Thugs want all your money!

If you don't want to pay Mogrul, your only alternative is to kill him, with the risk of the [Redoran Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") intervening to stop you. However, if you are observant of your surroundings while you are in Raven Rock, you can detect Mogrul and his bodyguard [Slitter](/wiki/Skyrim:Slitter "Skyrim:Slitter") approaching you to demand that you pay up if you haven't been informed of your debt yet. He will follow you out of town if you are patient and don't run too far ahead, allowing you to discreetly dispatch him without drawing the guards' ire.

You can also visit Drovas and inform him of Mogrul's harassment. While he will not be willing to pay the debt on his own initiative, you can persuade him to provide you with whatever money he can to help you pay off the debt. You must pass a hard [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") check to successfully persuade Drovas to give you the money. If you succeed, he will give you 250 gold, but that won't be enough to cover the debt. The rest is up to you.

Note that you need a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill of 75 to successfully persuade him:

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **You should pay me what you can. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"Well... I... Oh, fine. Here. This is all I have."* **Failed**: *"I don't see why. He's your problem now."* | **Passed**: Get 250 gold **Failed**: Nothing |

## Notes

- When Mogrul first approaches you for the initial conversation, exiting the conversation without picking a dialogue option will not start the quest. Mogrul will continue to follow, and attempt to initiate the same conversation again. You can lead Mogrul out of Raven Rock this way, allowing him to be killed without witnesses. Mogrul will not follow you into a building, or if you fast travel somewhere.
- If you attack Mogrul in the [Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") and [Teldryn Sero](/wiki/Skyrim:Teldryn_Sero "Skyrim:Teldryn Sero") either currently is (or has previously been) under your employ, Sero will come to your aid. If you previously finished [Unearthed](/wiki/Skyrim:Unearthed "Skyrim:Unearthed") and spared [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys"), Ralis will come to your aid as well.
- If you don't want to pay your debt but find it impossible to assassinate Mogrul without incurring a bounty, you can use [Nightingale Subterfuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Subterfuge "Skyrim:Nightingale Subterfuge"). Casting it while he, among others, is in its area of effect will result in them fighting, likely leading to Mogrul's death.
- Drovas will comment after the quest is finished, depending on your decision:
  - If you pay the debt, Drovas will say *"I heard you paid my debt to Mogrul. I don't know how I can every*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *repay you."*
  - If you kill Mogrul, Drovas will say *"I heard Mogrul is dead. That is a relief!"*
- After the quest is finished, you can pickpocket Mogrul to reclaim your money, but the gold may not be present in his inventory if you wait too long.

## Bugs

- If Mogrul is killed inside the Retching Netch while you are hidden, [Slitter](/wiki/Skyrim:Slitter "Skyrim:Slitter") will search for you. If you unhide so that he finds you and then attacks you and you flee outside, he will not follow you. Subsequently, even if you immediately re-enter the Retching Netch, Slitter will not be hostile to you, and will still tell you to talk to Mogrul.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Mogrul can still send thugs after you, even though this quest has been completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| A New Debt (DLC2TT1b) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | Someone named Mogrul sent a messenger for me. This Mogrul wants to talk. *Objective 100:* Talk to Mogrul |
| 200 |  | Helping Drovas has come back to bite me. He owed a money lender named Mogrul 1000 septims. Now Mogrul expects me to pay Drovas' debt. If I don't, he's going to keep sending thugs after me. *Objective 200:* Pay Mogrul |
| 300 | ☑ | Helping Drovas has come back to bite me. He owed a money lender named Mogrul 1000 septims. Mogrul expected me to pay Drovas debt, which I've done. |
| 310 | ☑ | Helping Drovas has come back to bite me. He owed a money lender named Mogrul 1000 septims. Mogrul expected me to pay Drovas debt. However, I killed him instead. |
| 320 | ☑ | Helping Drovas has come back to bite me. He owed a money lender named Mogrul 1000 septims. I persuaded him to take half that. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 210:* Pay or kill Mogrul |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 50.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TT1b stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TT1b`.

# Skyrim:A New Order

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").** |
