# Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Go where a [famous alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") could not in order to aid ground-breaking research.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Sinderion's Field Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Journal "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Journal") in his Field Laboratory, Blackreach *or* picking up a Crimson Nirnroot. |
| Location(s): | [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm") |
| Reward: | [Sinderion's Serendipity](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Serendipity "Skyrim:Sinderion's Serendipity") ability, *[The Nirnroot Missive](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Nirnroot_Missive "Skyrim:The Nirnroot Missive")* |
| ID: | NN01 |
| Suggested Level: | 18 |

A Crimson Nirnroot plant in [Sinderion's Field Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Laboratory "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Laboratory")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Collect thirty samples of the mysterious [Crimson Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot").
2. Take these samples to [Sinderion](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion")'s colleague [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi") so that Sinderion's research may continue.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Seemingly unreachable Crimson Nirnroot, which can be harvested with a [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint").

### The "Noisy Red Weed"

Sinderion had been obsessed with [Crimson Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") since purchasing a plant from a passing adventurer wanting to get something for the "noisy red weed" he found. Sinderion compensated the man, and then left [Skingrad](/wiki/Oblivion:Skingrad "Oblivion:Skingrad") to set up a laboratory in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), the only known habitat of Crimson Nirnroot.

### Continue the Research

The quest begins upon the collection of a sample crimson nirnroot in Blackreach. Your journal will update to reflect your part in finding out the significance of this plant. In order to get started, begin at the beginning in [Sinderion's Field Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Laboratory "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Laboratory"). The research facility is located in Blackreach, right across from the gates of [Alftand Cathedral](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"). Inside you will find Sinderion's remains still clutching his field journal. After reading the journal, the quest will update requesting that you collect thirty Crimson Nirnroot samples from Blackreach - a difficult but rewarding task.

### Locating the Samples

There are forty-four samples of Crimson Nirnroot within Blackreach (including some inside Blackreach's buildings). Unlike the more common [garden variety Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), the Crimson Nirnroot does not solely grow near bodies of water. Many plants are found near patches of mushrooms, Dwemer pipes or along the sides of the cavern. Since there are forty-four plants, all required samples can be collected at one time if you thoroughly explore Blackreach (see the [Crimson Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") article for more details on plant locations). Alternatively, if you are having a hard time finding enough plants, they will respawn. Leaving Blackreach for ten days allows you to collect another sample from any previously-harvested plants.

### A Job Well Done

After collecting the required number of plants, the quest will update again and you will be asked to deliver them to [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi"), Sinderion's former colleague. She is currently residing at [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm"), between [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and  [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").
Give Avrusa the thirty Crimson Nirnroot samples to complete the quest and receive *[The Nirnroot Missive](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Nirnroot_Missive "Skyrim:The Nirnroot Missive")*. You will also be provided with [Sinderion's Serendipity](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Serendipity "Skyrim:Sinderion's Serendipity"), an [ability](/wiki/Skyrim:Abilities "Skyrim:Abilities") which provides a 25% chance to mix two potions instead of one.

## Notes

- The [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") perk [Green Thumb](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Thumb "Skyrim:Green Thumb") does not affect Nirnroot and therefore cannot be used to decrease the number of plants needed to be harvested.
- The quest is a sequel to the [Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion") quest, [Seeking Your Roots](/wiki/Oblivion:Seeking_Your_Roots "Oblivion:Seeking Your Roots").
- While this quest is active and toggled on in the quests log, the spell [Clairvoyance](/wiki/Skyrim:Clairvoyance "Skyrim:Clairvoyance") will determine that the Dragonborn is the closest quest marker, making Clairvoyance less useful. Toggling the quest off mitigates this issue.

## Bugs

- The counter for the number of Crimson Nirnroots in your inventory may not function properly, resulting in a number of related issues:
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - if you consume all the Crimson Nirnroot in your inventory, not only will that amount be redacted from the quest counter, but the counter will even count the removed roots twice, potentially causing the counter to go into the negatives.
  - The quest may update telling you to return the nirnroot and stating you have found 30 samples when you have actually found less. Once you have the required amount, you will be able to return it and the quest should continue as normal.
  - Once all thirty Crimson Nirnroots have been collected the option to give them to Avrusa is not there, thus freezing the quest.
    - Simply drop one and pick it back up to continue the quest.
  - If you place Crimson Nirnroot in a container or follower's inventory, or otherwise remove it from your inventory, the appropriate number may or may not be removed from the quest log.
    - To complete the quest even if the quest log does not represent the actual amount of Crimson Nirnroot you have in inventory simply go to Avrusa with thirty in your inventory, and the quest will complete itself without updating in the journal.
    - The number of Crimson Nirnroot in the quest log is thrown off if you transfer them to or from a container in groups. If you place more than one in a container at one time the quest log will think you only moved one. The quest log number can be corrected by placing them in a container and pulling them out individually (e.g., it says you have nine but you have ten: place two in a container at one time, and then pull them out one at a time). You can also get the quest log up to 30/30 with this method, but you cannot complete the quest without thirty in your inventory.
    -  To fix the count directly, use the console commands: `set NN01Count to amount` and `UpdateQuestInstanceGlobal NN01 NN01Count` . Note that this will not cause the quest to advance if set directly to 30. To do so, drop one and pick it up again.
- Certain samples of the Crimson Nirnroot can in very rare cases be impossible to pick up and added to your inventory. **?**
  - This bug can be fixed by reloading a previous save. If reloading does not work, you can try picking up other samples of the Crimson Nirnroot.

## Quest Stages

| A Return To Your Roots (NN01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |

| 15 |  | I've discovered an unusual ingredient called Crimson Nirnroot. *Objective 5:* Discover the significance of Crimson Nirnroot |
| 20 |  | I've discovered the remains of Sinderion, an alchemist from Skingrad in Cyrodiil. He was exploring Blackreach in search of the Crimson Nirnroot, and appeared to be on the brink of an amazing discovery. *Objective 10:* Collect Crimson Nirnroot in Blackreach (<Global=NN01Count>/30) |
|  |  | *(Upon collecting the thirtieth Crimson Nirnroot)* *Objective 20:* Bring 30 Crimson Nirnroot to Avrusa Sarethi |
| 200 | ☑ | I have brought my Crimson Nirnroot to Avrusa Sarethi, a former student of Sinderion. She was overjoyed that I was able to complete Sinderion's field work and pledged to continue his research in his memory. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage NN01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest NN01`.

# Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Help [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") trace her roots in [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") |
| Location(s): | [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") |
| Reward: | [Spell Tome: Conjure Flaming Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Flaming_Familiar "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Flaming Familiar"), [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs"), Word for the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") shout,  [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(item) "Skyrim:Vokun (item)") |
| ID: | dunHighGateRuinsQST |
| Suggested Level: | 24 |

[High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Meet and talk to [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") in [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") and agree to help her.
2. Protect Anska as you fight through the ruins.
3. Defeat [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)").
4. Retrieve Anska's [scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealed_Scroll "Skyrim:Sealed Scroll").

### Anska

[High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") is a remote [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") on the snowy tundra east of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), near the shores of the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"). When you enter, it soon becomes clear that someone visited the ruin recently, as the residing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") have already been killed. Proceed into the first room and you will meet the person responsible, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") named [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska"). When approached she will introduce herself and ask if you are there to help her as she has finally located [Vokun's](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)") Crypt. She then explains her goal, namely to locate a special scroll that could link her family blood all the way back to the legendary [Ysgramor](/wiki/Lore:Ysgramor "Lore:Ysgramor"). She will also briefly describe Vokun as *"Some old priest buried here long ago."*, hinting at her lack of research and explaining her need for help. She fears the old priest could awaken and prove too powerful a foe, so she wants you to lead her through the ruin and help her fight the opposition. Accept her request and the quest will start.

### High Gate Ruins

*"Sometimes I just like to watch them burn."*

Anska is not your average [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") and you will have to escort her safely through the ruin; she is, however, capable of taking care of herself using a variety of leveled wizard spells, so keep an eye out and stay upfront as you proceed into the dungeon. Take the northern tunnel to a huge chamber infested with leveled draugr. Claim some minor loot from the chest in the alcove, then head upstairs and locate the iron door leading north where three more draugr will attack. Go through the room with the [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and a few useful potions. The next tunnel contains a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") triggering a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall"), so make sure Anska gets through unharmed. A lever puzzle awaits in the next room, so take a thorough look at the [symbols](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Puzzle_Doors "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") above the southern ledge. From left to right, they are: **Eagle—Whale—Fox—Snake**. Look around the room for the levers, all of them on pedestals with corresponding symbols. The two first levers are upstairs while the last two are on the ground floor. When all four levers are pulled in the right order, the grate in the middle of the room will disappear, so head downstairs and enter the [catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins_Catacombs "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins Catacombs") through the door.

Only one draugr will attack you in the first section of the catacombs and a slide will lead you down to another catacomb area with more draugr. A chest can be found in an alcove, but watch out for the pressure plate and the corresponding [darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). Before long, you will reach a room with a leveled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") resting on a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"), which releases two draugr from the adjacent coffins if triggered. The locked door to the right contains a chest behind it. Continue into a hallway filled with ancient carvings and numerous pressure plates on the floor, triggering darts or [spear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap"), then proceed into another puzzle room. Facing the lever, two stone walls cover hidden doors, so pull the lever and watch the wall to the right disappear, then fight the boss-leveled draugr guarding another lever. Pull that lever and the door to the left will open and release yet another boss-leveled draugr. Pull the lever behind him, then head through the now-opened entrance to the east and into [Vokun's throne room](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun%27s_Throne_Room "Skyrim:Vokun's Throne Room").

### Vokun

Anska vs. [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)")

Before the throne room, a hallway offers a few potions. As soon as you open the next door, the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") Vokun will burst out of his sarcophagus and use his [staff of fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs") to attack you from a distance. Anska will keep her distance from Vokun, but will use her ranged attacks to help out. Defeat the priest and claim his unique [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(item) "Skyrim:Vokun (item)") and his staff from the remains. Proceed to the chamber to the east, where you will find a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") with a word for the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") [Shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). The nearby table holds the [sealed scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealed_Scroll "Skyrim:Sealed Scroll") for Anska, so pick it up and hand it to her. She will be overwhelmed with joy and hand you the unique spell tome for learning the spell [Conjure Flaming Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Flaming_Familiar "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Flaming Familiar") as a reward. Additionally, a boss-leveled chest can be found on the upper level to the north, in an alcove right next to the shortcut back to the first zone of the ruin. Anska will stay behind and try to decipher the scroll indefinitely.

## Notes

- Be careful about bringing other followers with you, since Anska's use of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic can cause them to attack her if she hits them by mistake, or if they hit her.
- This quest only counts towards the [Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") if Anska survives.
- Should you choose not to hand over the scroll to Anska right away, she'll continue to follow you around, but only within close proximity to the ruins. In other words, she can't be used as a "free" follower. If you withhold the scroll from her and head outside, then later give her the scroll, she will return to the ruins and remain in Vokun's throne room indefinitely.
- It is possible to clear the dungeon without [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska")'s help. To do this, avoid talking to her when you enter the dungeon. Once Vokun is dead, she will run up to you and allow for the quest to finish normally.
- Anska is not considered an essential NPC, and can be killed prior to starting the quest. This prevents the start of the quest and the acquisition of the [Flaming Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Flaming_Familiar "Skyrim:Flaming Familiar") spell.
- Area of effect spells such as [Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Fire Storm") or [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") can cause objects, including the scroll, to fly around the room, potentially becoming lost.

## Bugs

- On entering the Catacombs, Anska will comment on the soul gem well before you reach it, and before it is in your line of sight.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- Similarly, she may comment on Vokun's presence and the scroll beyond him ("There it is! On the table!"), before the door to his throne room is even open. **?**
- You may be stuck with the sealed scroll, should you pick it up after failing the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Upon killing Vokun, Anska may just stand in battle pose, not finishing the quest.
  -  This can be fixed by opening the console, targeting Anska, and using the `recycleactor` command. She will then vanish, re-enter the room, run toward Vokun's tomb, and you can now speak to her.
- The scroll may be left in your inventory after you complete the quest (you can remove it at that stage though, since it is no longer a quest item).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Leaving the reward room without taking the scroll will lead you to be locked out of the room. Even if you return to the throne room, the gates will be locked and cannot be opened anymore since the priest is already dead.
- If Anska is killed, the quest does not fail.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| A Scroll For Anska (dunHighGateRuinsQST) | | |

| 90 |  | I have the scroll, I should return it to Anska for my reward. |
| 100 | ☑ | High Gate Ruins is clear and Anska has rewarded me with a powerful new fire spell. |
| 150 | ☒ | I have failed to protect Anska, now I'll never know what her scroll was for. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 10:* Find And Return Anska's Scroll To Her  *Objective 20:* Help Anska Retrieve Her Scroll  *Objective 90:* Return The Scroll To Anska |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 30, 80, 110.

  Notes
- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunHighGateRuinsQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunHighGateRuinsQST`.

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst_(quest) "Skyrim:Bloodthirst (quest)") | | |

Beneath the city of Riften lies a dark secret...

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter the Ratway and follow the [Ghostly Apparition](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Ghostly_Apparition&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Ghostly Apparition (page does not exist)").
2. Investigate the [Vault](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Vault "Skyrim:The Guardian Vault").
3. Defeat [The Guardian](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:The_Guardian&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:The Guardian (page does not exist)") and see if it has affected the shield.
4. Head to the north chamber and defeat the Guardian again.
5. Head to the east chamber and defeat the Guardian again.
6. Return to the sword chamber.

## Detailed Walkthrough

As soon as you install the Dawnfang and Duskfang Creation, head to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Townsfolk are talking about a ghost hiding in the Ratway and guards have [warned them](/wiki/Skyrim:Public_Notice "Skyrim:Public Notice") not to approach the area. As you begin your search, a ghostly apparition appears to guide you throughout the Ratway to the Guardian Vault. She then disappears in front of the [Guardian Vault](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Vault "Skyrim:The Guardian Vault"), leaving you to your investigation.

In the chamber, you find a long dead skeleton and a sword. Upon inspecting the latter, the Vault Guardian tries to stop you and you have to defeat him. His death seems to have weakened the shield protecting the sword, and a door opens to the north. Head there to find once more the Vault Guardian and weaken the shield. Before leaving the northern room, be sure to open the cages to the left of the upper platform. Behind the gate there sits the skeleton of Verrick Tilwald, which will reanimate and attack you as you enter. Once the skeleton is dispatched, take [Verrick's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Verrick%27s_Note "Skyrim:Verrick's Note"), which is pinned beneath a dagger on the table next to [Of Crossed Daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Crossed_Daggers "Skyrim:Of Crossed Daggers"). Reading this will initiate the [Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst_(quest) "Skyrim:Bloodthirst (quest)") quest.
Return to the sword chamber and head to the east, defeat the Vault Guardian for the last time.

The Guardian and the Ghostly Apparition, in life Lorant and Emma Bouchard, will be reunited and you'll be free to take [Dawnfang and Duskfang](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang").

## Notes

- For historical information on Dawnfang & Duskfang, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Dawnfang_and_Duskfang "Lore:Dawnfang and Duskfang").
- It is possible to yield to Lorant's final form once he appears non-magical, at which time he simply stands in place peaceably with arms outstretched, effectively pausing the battle.

## Bugs

- It may be impossible to loot Lorant's corpse. **?**
- The game may crash when the second Guardian dies.
- If you kill all enemies in the north chamber boss room except the north chamber's guardian, he may stop being hostile. **?**
-   On the way to the north chamber, one of the three skeletons found at the bottom of the staircase may always be named "Cursed Smuggler" despite the game being in a language that is not English. **?**
- The two skeletons sitting beside the coffin may become immortal if you attack them before touching the coffin. They should revert to normal after touching the coffin. **?**

{{Bug|On console in the east room when you defeat the red guardian the green guardian might not spawn.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE013_AquisitionQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE013_AquisitionQuest`.

# Skyrim:Abandoned Building

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Abandoned Building ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Abandoned+Building)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2RRAbandonedBuilding | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") | |

Abandoned Building

The **Abandoned Building** is the home of [Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel") and [Rirns Llervu](/wiki/Skyrim:Rirns_Llervu "Skyrim:Rirns Llervu") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is on the waterfront west of [Glover Mallory's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House"), being the last building on the waterfront along the path to the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone") to the west. Until the stone is cleansed during the quest [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), the building is uninhabited. After the stone is cleansed, Bralsa Drel and Rirns Llervu will take residence.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel")  [Rirns Llervu](/wiki/Skyrim:Rirns_Llervu "Skyrim:Rirns Llervu") |

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance are two unusable barrels. To the right of the entrance is a lit brazier and three [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants. Along the back of the building on the waterfront are three crates and more unusable barrels. The entrance is unlocked.

### Abandoned Building

First room

Second room

Upper floor

The entrance leads into a squalid building littered with ash piles, cobwebs, and [tankards](/wiki/Skyrim:Tankard "Skyrim:Tankard") and other minor items messily strewn about. In the middle of the room is a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on the floor. In the southeast corner is another bottle of Nord mead on an ash pile. Along the west wall is a sideboard holding a bottle of Nord mead, a bottle of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"), a copy of *[Confessions of a Dunmer Skooma Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Confessions_of_a_Dunmer_Skooma_Eater "Skyrim:Confessions of a Dunmer Skooma Eater")*, and a bottle of [matze](/wiki/Skyrim:Matze "Skyrim:Matze"), with a copy of *[The Poison Song, Book IV](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_IV "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book IV")* on the wall ledge behind the dresser. Along the north wall is another bottle of matze on the wall ledge, a doorway to the next room, and two more bottles of Nord mead on the wall ledge and a crate, respectively.

The next room is circular, and features the stairs leading up to the upper floor. Along the curved west wall are two owned bed rolls, with a bottle of [flin](/wiki/Skyrim:Flin "Skyrim:Flin"), a bottle of sujamma, a bottle of [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a wedge of [goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") between them, and a crate holding another loaf of bread and a copy of *[The Five Far Stars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Five_Far_Stars "Skyrim:The Five Far Stars")*. Along the north wall beneath the stairs are two ingredient urns and an unusable barrel. The small circular room on the upper floor contains two sacks, a meat barrel, three unusable barrels, and four crates.

# Skyrim:Abandoned House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Abandoned House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MarkarthAbandonedHouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | |
| Special Features | |
| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Empty](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Empty") Empty |

The Abandoned House in Markarth

The **Abandoned House** is a building in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") next to [Arnleif and Sons Trading Company](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company") with a shrine to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal").

Although abandoned, the house is fully furnished. It has four rooms and a tunnel in the basement leading to the shrine.

## Related Quests

- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Abandoned House

Shrine of Molag Bal in the Abandoned House

The front door opens to a spacious, multipurpose room. A shelving unit just to the right of the front door holds a [Potion of True Shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot") and a [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt"), as well as some [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Right next to the cupboard is an unlocked chest containing leveled items. A selection of [iron weaponry](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") is displayed on the adjacent table, together with more wine and alto wine. However, any of these items may become dislodged during the first stages of the related quest, and subsequently found on the floor nearby. The nearby dresser is a safe storage option, but contains only clothes. A mace is sitting on top.

The other side of the room serves as a kitchen and dining area. While the spit over the fire is not usable, plenty of foodstuffs can be found in this area, both on the table and scattered on the floor. A basket with two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") is by the front door. A small round table around the corner holds a bottle of wine, a bottle of alto wine, and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). A dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braids "Skyrim:Garlic Braids"), and a dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam") are hanging to the left of the fire, with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on a pile of wood below. To the right of the fireplace are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), along with an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), and another cabbage. The cupboard to the right holds only tableware and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), but is a safe storage option. The table is laden with food: two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a serving of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a sliced eidar cheese, an eidar cheese wedge, two loaves and a piece of bread, two bottles of alto wine, and a bottle of wine. A second unlocked chest by the table contains leveled items. The end table has clutter, but is another safe storage option.

The second room is furnished with a usable bed. A hidden chest containing leveled items is tucked underneath the foot of the bed. More safe storage options are in the bedroom, including the end table by the bed and the dresser across from the bed. A bottle of wine is on the end table, and a bottle of alto wine and a cheap book are on the dresser. The cupboard is also safe, and holds a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), an iron sword, and a sabre cat pelt. A copy of *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* may be found under the cupboard. An unlocked chest by the doorway to the next room contains leveled items.

The next room and lower levels of the house are used mostly for storage. A small coin purse, clutched by a skeletal arm, is on the pillar at the foot of the stairs. To the left is a shelving unit containing clutter, a bottle of wine, a bottle of alto wine, and two loaves of bread. Two rabbits, a pheasant, a dried elves ear, and a garlic braid hang straight ahead on the west wall, near another potato and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") on a barrel. To the right is a wall shelf with some sacks, a loaf of bread, and a goat cheese wheel. In the northeast corner is a cupboard containing clutter and two potatoes. Next to the cupboard is a wall shelf with more sacks. The furniture is safe storage, but contains nothing of interest. Before the next room is a small area with a wall shelf containing clutter, more sacks, and a barrel, with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the floor.

The next room down contains a desk ahead with a bottle of wine, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a barrel containing more Nord mead. To the left are four more barrels, three of which contain more Nord mead. There is a shelving unit to the left of the barrels containing clutter, some sacks, two bottles of alto wine, and two bottles of wine. In the remaining half of the room are four more shelving units containing clutter, sacks, another bottle of alto wine, and another pickaxe, with five more barrels nearby, three containing Nord mead. When exploring the room, you will notice a draft coming from the south. Following this leads you to a tunnel heading down. The tunnel winds through some [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") ruins to the shrine of Molag Bal. The only item of slight interest in the tunnel is another pickaxe.

## Notes

- The house can be used as free player housing, as items will not disappear from the containers.
- There are no cooking, alchemy, or enchanting facilities, but the house has the largest amount of storage containers in the game, with 62 in total.
- The poltergeist effect that triggers as part of the House of Horrors can be avoided in order to keep the house tidy. If [Vigilant Tyranus](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Tyranus "Skyrim:Vigilant Tyranus") is killed before the effect starts, it will never occur, and all furniture will remain positioned normally, while the quest will proceed without problems.
  - The effect causes the chairs in the entrance room to become rearranged atop the table. If this happens and you prefer the old arrangement, the chairs can be reset by activating the console and typing `prid c2527` followed by `disable`.
- A copy of the book *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* can be found under a cupboard in the second room after you reach level 30, leading to another Daedric quest.
- There is an "Empty" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") at the bottom left of the entrance door, due to the lack of notable loot inside.
- The house is referred to as [Logrolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Logrolf_the_Willful "Skyrim:Logrolf the Willful")'s House in the Creation Kit.
- The house is [occupied by seemingly normal people](/wiki/Online:Etavarn%27s_House "Online:Etavarn's House") in *[The Elder Scrolls Online](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online"): [Markarth](/wiki/Online:Markarth_(DLC) "Online:Markarth (DLC)")*. The altar to Molag Bal didn't yet exist at that time.

## Bugs

- Tyranus can go missing from his usual location outside the building. If this occurs, he may reappear near the stables outside of the city.
- The scene between Yngvar and Tyranus in front of the building that introduces The House of Horrors may cause Yngvar to warp back from Windhelm if he was exiled to there as a result of the Civil War.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

The Abandoned Lodge

The **Abandoned Lodge** is a small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Places#Shacks "Skyrim:Dragonborn Places") north-northeast of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). It contains only one zone, *[Abandoned Lodge](#Abandoned_Lodge)*.

It is an old hunting lodge built in the traditional Nordic style common in Skyrim. It contains little of importance except during the quest [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim"). Prior to starting the quest, the door is [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Abandoned_Lodge "Skyrim:Key to Abandoned Lodge")-locked; you will be unable to enter until the quest has started.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") [†](#intnote_rq) [‡](#intnote_leaves)  [Thalmor Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Thalmor") [†](#intnote_rq) |

[†](#note_rq)Appear after starting the related quest.

[‡](#note_leaves)Returns to [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") after completing the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim")**: Find a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") missing from [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

### Exterior

In front of the entrance is a campfire, three [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes, a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"), a meat barrel, two empty barrels, three sacks, and two crates. Along the northeast wall are two more bear traps, a meat barrel, an empty barrel, four sacks, three crates, two [snow bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Bear Pelt"), and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"). To the left of the entrance is an empty barrel and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). To the right of the entrance is a meat barrel, an empty barrel, two sacks, and a crate. Once the related quest has begun, four hostile [Thalmor soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Thalmor"), one of whom carries the key to the lodge, will be on guard outside.

### Abandoned Lodge

The first floor

The entrance leads into a derelict building strewn with debris and cobwebs. In the southeast corner is a single bed. In the northeast corner are three snow bear pelts, a wardrobe, and two chairs and a table holding five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a copy of *[A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Gentleman%27s_Guide_to_Whiterun "Skyrim:A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun")*. Along the north wall is a double bed with an empty [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at its foot, an unlit fireplace, and a wood pile. Along the south wall are three chairs, one of which is overturned, a table, a set of shelves with two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids hanging above the shelves, and an unusable barrel. Along the west wall are the stairs down to the basement.

The basement

During the related quest, the kidnapped [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") is found in the southeast corner of the basement. Along the south wall is an unusable barrel, a table, and a wood pile. Along the east wall is a food barrel, an unusable barrel, a set of shelves holding a bear trap, three [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), and two snow bear pelts, a novice-locked chest, and a wood pile. Along the north wall is a set of shelves and a bar counter holding two salt piles, a piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a chair and a small round table holding another piece of bread, with a garlic braid hanging from the ceiling near the table. In the northwest corner beneath the stairs is a bear trap, three sacks, an unusable barrel, three crates, and three [deer pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt").

## Notes

- The Thalmor soldiers at the lodge differ from their [counterparts](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") in Skyrim, as they wear [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor") instead of the [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Armor "Skyrim:Elven Armor") or [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Armor "Skyrim:Glass Armor") armor worn by other Thalmor. However, their [helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") are all elven, with a chance of them being standard Elven, Elven Light, or a mix of the two.
- The Thalmor soldiers continue to respawn even after the quest is completed. However, the new soldiers will not be hostile. If you decide to engage them in combat they will become hostile, but there are no repercussions for killing them.
- The design of the lodge's interior is strikingly similar to [Alvor and Sigrid's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor_and_Sigrid%27s_House "Skyrim:Alvor and Sigrid's House").

# Skyrim:Abandoned Prison

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Imperial Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Imperial_Tower.png) | Imperial Tower: Abandoned Prison ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+Prison)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Song of Hrormir](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_Of_Hrormir "Skyrim:Song Of Hrormir")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| AbandonedPrisonExterior01, AbandonedPrison01 | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| Southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") North-northwest of [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol") | |

Abandoned Prison

The **Abandoned Prison** is a small [Imperial prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing the [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") of its drowned prisoners. It contains only one zone, *[Abandoned Prison](#Abandoned_Prison)*.

## Walkthrough

Prison exit

### Exterior

There are two entrances into the abandoned prison. The first is the marked main entrance located along the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") as you approach [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol"). The second is a hidden exit underneath the bridge along the river just east of the main entrance. It is not possible to explore the entire prison if you enter via the hatch under the bridge due to a one-way drop inside the prison. There is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the top of the tower directly above the main entrance. It can be reached by crossing the river by [Lucky Lorenz](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucky_Lorenz "Skyrim:Lucky Lorenz")'s crushed house, walking along the bank, and then climbing the hillside to the left of the tower. On the riverbank opposite the main entrance is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein").

### Abandoned Prison

One of the blocks of cells

One of the guard rooms

The trapdoor exit

The main entrance leads directly into the second level of a circular tower. Rubble blocks the stairs leading up to higher levels to the left. There is plenty of [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") to be harvested on the two accessible floors of the tower. Stairs on the right spiral down to a passage and circular room that have also suffered extensive damage, with water seeping in and partially flooding the room. There are several crates, barrels, and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks around the walls. Against the wall of the passage is a tall wardrobe containing random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with an unlocked chest on top. To the left is an open door and passage heading north. To the left of this is a wooden table with another food sack on and under it. In the center of the circular room, among some rubble is an open chest with an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), a [Solution of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Solution of Regeneration"), and a [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison") inside. Against the west wall is a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") sitting on a crate next to a food barrel. To the northwest is a doorway that originally led to more stairs leading down; however, these are also blocked by a cave-in.

Head north through the open door down some stairs to a guard room. The table in front of you holds only a few cheap pieces of crockery. There is an unlocked gate to the left leading into a long, narrow room that was used for storage. It contains a set of shelves that are leaning against the wall and another set holding a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"), a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a fillet of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"), and a food sack. To the left of this is a row of three weapon racks holding an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") and an [Imperial bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow"), with an [Imperial shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Shield") leaning against a stack of crates with a bowl of [apple cabbage stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Cabbage_Stew "Skyrim:Apple Cabbage Stew") on top. At the back of the room is a small table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and the [guard's orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Orders "Skyrim:Guard's Orders") to kill or let the prisoners drown and for the guards to evacuate the prison.

To the east is another flight of stairs leading to a small room, with passages to the north and south that are partially blocked with fallen beams and masonry, allowing you to look through to other areas that are unreachable from here. To the north a [ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") is wandering up and down a passage to the room you can see. You can either snipe them from here or leave them for later. There is a dresser containing a mix of common and [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), with a pair of [Imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots") on top. In the southwest corner are two sets of shelves. One holds a pair of [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and cheap crockery. The other holds three [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), four [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), one of them hidden in a bowl, a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), and a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots").

To the east is another flight of stairs leading down to the start of the cells. Two ghosts inhabit this room. One ghost is in the second cell on the south side of the room. This cell door is wide open. The second ghost is in the third cell on the north side of the room. This cell door is expert-locked, so you can either unlock it or fire through the bars to deal with this ghost. Both will try to attack when alerted to your presence. The room has a raised central passage with rows of cells and lower paths on either side. On your immediate right as you enter the room are the skeletal remains of one of the prisoners; an Imperial sword and shield lie beside the skeleton, along with a note detailing the [prisoner's plan](/wiki/Skyrim:Prisoner%27s_Plan "Skyrim:Prisoner's Plan") to attack the guards and escape through the drainage grate. The first cell to the south is empty except for a couple crates. The second contains a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and bedroll in addition to the ghost. The third contains a bedroll and an open trapdoor leading to the drains and leads to the escape route mentioned in the note—a flooded passageway that gives access to the secret exit underneath the bridge. Once you drop through the trapdoor, you will not be able to climb back up to the jail cells, so it is advisable to leave exploration of this area until you have finished exploring the rest of the prison. The first cell on the north side contains two skeletons and a bedroll. The second is expert-locked and only contains a bedroll. The third contains a bedroll and a large hole in the wall leading to another cell-filled room. At the east end of the room is another skeleton next to a table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a small coin purse, and the [Abandoned Prison Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Prison_Key "Skyrim:Abandoned Prison Key") on it that opens all of the locked cells in the prison as well as the master-locked chest in the warden's quarters. If you wish to hone your [lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill, leave this key behind.

Through the hole to the north is another room with a row of three more expert-locked cells. Each cell contains one or two bedrolls, but only the last of the three contains a skeleton. All of the skeletons in both rooms can be looted for a few gold and/or [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"). At the eastern end of the passage between the row of cells and a raised passage is a food barrel and an unlocked chest on top of a crate. At the western end of the lower passage is a large vat. On the higher passage, at the eastern end is a wardrobe containing clothes and four food sacks among a couple of crates. Continuing to the west you'll pass a table and a wall shelf, which hold cheap crockery, and a wooden bench. At the far end, stairs lead up to the warden's quarters. If you didn't deal with the first ghost through the cave-in, then this is where you'll have to face it. On your left is an unowned single bed, a wardrobe containing random clothes, and a small table with a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a medium coin purse, and four loose septims on top. Opposite, to the west is an overturned end table partially buried in rubble, an unlocked chest, a potion of minor magicka, and a [leather helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"). A skeleton with an Imperial sword and shield lies on the floor in the middle of the room. To the south the passage is blocked, but on the right is a doorway to another long, narrow storeroom. At the northern end is a master-locked chest, which is opened with the same key as the one that opened the cells, and on the floor in front is a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Song of Hrormir](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_Of_Hrormir "Skyrim:Song Of Hrormir")*. There are also two sets of shelves holding thirteen [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), some cheap crockery, and four [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot").

You can now exit the prison through the trapdoor in the southeast prison cell or backtrack to the main entrance. Dropping down the drain, the tunnel leads west before turning south and opening out to a normal-sized passage. It then turns west again and continues to a T-junction, where you'll find another skeleton and a food barrel with a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") on top. The passage ahead is caved-in, so your only option is to turn south. At the end is a ladder leading to the alternative exit. The skeletons scattered around the hatch under the bridge provide more evidence of the prisoners' ill-fated escape attempt.

## Notes

- The prison is across the river from [Treasure Map IX](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_IX "Skyrim:Treasure Map IX") on Lucky Lorenz's corpse. His collapsed house can be seen from the top of the crumbling prison tower.
- East of the prison cells there is a room that can only be reached on the PC by using the 'tcl' console command. The room has no doors, and contains a bucket, a basket, a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a mug, and a chest.
- The many locked doors and chests provide a good opportunity to increase your Lockpicking skill.

## Bugs

- Fast traveling to the Abandoned Prison with a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") may cause that follower to appear on the riverbank opposite the prison's main entrance, with no way of crossing the river itself.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Followers may be unable to enter or exit the Abandoned Prison through either of the prison's entrances.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  -  Followers may be moved inside the prison using the console. Once you are inside, use `prid <actor ID>` (where <actor ID> is the follower's RefID) and then `moveto player` to select and move the follower next to you. Followers moved inside the prison in this manner will need to be moved back outside afterward due to their inability to follow you through either exit.
- The ghosts here incorrectly drop physical loot despite being otherwise setup to be ghosts who shouldn't do that. They may also disintegrate into the wrong kind of ash piles when killed.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.6, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Abandoned Prison

# Skyrim:Abandoned Shack

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shack.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shack.png) | Shack: Abandoned Shack ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+Shack)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| NPCs | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Blade of Woe](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Woe "Skyrim:Blade of Woe") (see [notes](#Notes)) | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| AbandonedShackExterior, AbandonedShackInterior | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| East-southeast of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | |

The Abandoned Shack

The **Abandoned Shack** is an isolated [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), east of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

This is where you will awaken the first time you sleep after completing [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost") and receiving the [mysterious note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(DB) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (DB)"). The quest [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") will automatically start upon awakening. This is also where you can instead begin [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") by killing [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid"), which will cause the previous quest to fail. The shack cannot be accessed before this point, as the door is locked and requires a key; however, it remains unlocked after you leave it.

## Related Quests

- **[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")**: Repay your debt to [the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and show you are willing to kill on command.
- **[Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")**: Finish the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") and rid Skyrim of their kind.

## Exterior

There are two barrels and a crate either side of the door. A few feet to the southwest is a rowboat and a crate. There are blood splatters on the door. The following plants are found on the same island as the shack:

| Plants |
| --- |
| 5 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell")  3 [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade")  2 [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root")  1 [Spiky Grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") |

## Abandoned Shack

The shack's interior

Upon awakening in the shack, you will see in the southwest corner an empty set of shelves with Astrid sitting on top. Against the west wall is an empty, unlocked chest, a small cage, an empty dresser, and another set of shelves. The north wall has a cart, an empty barrel, a fireplace with piles of firewood on either side, and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") in front. Against the east wall are three kneeling prisoners—[Fultheim the Fearless](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim_the_Fearless "Skyrim:Fultheim the Fearless"), [Alea Quintus](/wiki/Skyrim:Alea_Quintus "Skyrim:Alea Quintus"), and [Vasha](/wiki/Skyrim:Vasha "Skyrim:Vasha")—with their hands bound and their faces covered by [execution hoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Execution_Hood "Skyrim:Execution Hood"). There is another small cage in the southeast corner. There is a locked door (key required) in the center of the south wall, which leads outside. To the left is a bench, some more firewood, and a chair, while to the right is a mead barrel and a sack. Towards the middle of the room is an unowned single bed with a small table next to it. There is blood splattered over the south, east and west walls. You must kill at least one of the prisoners (or Astrid) in order to get the key either by being given it by Astrid or by taking it off her body. The map marker for the shack is only added after either Astrid gives you the key or you kill Astrid and loot it from her corpse, unless you have already found it prior to being brought here. The shack will remain uninhabited, aside from the corpses of anyone you killed.

## Notes

- South-southeast of the shack is a hilltop with seven stone pillars, marking the ruins of some forgotten structure. Scattered about the ruins are a burial urn, a novice-locked chest, and the body of a [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") containing a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Sacred Witness](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacred_Witness "Skyrim:Sacred Witness")*. The chest is found behind some rubble, underneath a twisted tree. The burial urn and draugr are on the opposite side of the collapsed pillar, behind the chest. Two [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") veins can be found nearby.
- The [Blade of Woe](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Woe "Skyrim:Blade of Woe") and a full set of Shrouded equipment ([Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor"), [Shrouded Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Shrouded Gloves"), [Shrouded Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Boots "Skyrim:Shrouded Boots"), [Shrouded Cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl")) can be obtained by killing Astrid if you choose not to join the Brotherhood.

## Bugs

- Installing [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") may cause a bad navmesh inside the Abandoned Shack, which disconnects the door.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- If When Friends Like These... is set to transport you here while [The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan") is about to begin, that quest would be interrupted and potentially broken by the kidnapping scene.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, addresses this issue. The fact that these happen to be the only two quests in the vanilla game that require you to sleep is likely why this went unnoticed for so long.

# Skyrim:Abelone

## Overview

| Abelone (RefID: 00087750) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | | |
| Location | [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00087750 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0008774F |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 75 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 60 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 60 | | |

| Voice Type | [FemaleCommoner](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionPale](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionPale "Skyrim:CrimeFactionPale"); [DawnstarWindpeakInnFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DawnstarWindpeakInnFaction "Skyrim:DawnstarWindpeakInnFaction"); [TownDawnstarFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownDawnstarFaction "Skyrim:TownDawnstarFaction") | | |

Abelone

**Abelone** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who lives and works at the [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

Her workday is divided between carrying firewood and doing various duties outside the Windpeak Inn. At 7am she will carry firewood for two hours and at 9am she will either lean against the fence of the chicken pen, use the [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), or chop wood at the [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). At 11am she returns to carrying firewood until she eats a one-hour breakfast on the bench at noon. At 1pm she returns to her random duties until 3pm when she spends another two hours carrying firewood. Her workday ends with yet another two hours of random duties until 7pm when she sits down on the bench for a one-hour dinner. The evening is spent inside the inn, socializing with the regulars. At 11pm she was supposed to go to bed for seven hours, and wake up to a one-hour breakfast at 6am, but doesn't, due to a [bug](#Bugs).

She wears a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"), a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes"), and a [cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Cowl "Skyrim:Cowl"). She carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") to defend herself.

## Dialogue

Speaking to Abelone while she is working outside will have her suggest that you head inside the inn:

:   *"I work for the Windpeak Inn. You should head on inside."*
:   *"[Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring "Skyrim:Thoring") runs the inn. Speak to him."*

## Bugs

- Abelone was supposed to eat a one-hour breakfast at 6am but the package was accidentally set to noon.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12478))
- Abelone was supposed to sleep inside the Windpeak between 11pm and 6am, but her sleep package is not of the correct type.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
