# Skyrim:About

## Overview

Collector's Edition box art

***[The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")***, the fifth game in the *[Elder Scrolls](/wiki/General:The_Elder_Scrolls "General:The Elder Scrolls")* series, takes place in the province of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") 200 years after the [Oblivion Crisis](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion_Crisis "Lore:Oblivion Crisis").[[1]](#cite_note-FebGI-1) [Dragons](/wiki/Lore:Dragon "Lore:Dragon") and their [language](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Language "Lore:Dragon Language") play an integral role in the story.[[2]](#cite_note-2)

The High King of Skyrim has been murdered, triggering a civil war among the province's people, the [Nords](/wiki/Lore:Nord "Lore:Nord"). Many Nords wish to secede from the empire, which has been declining in power since the fall of the [Septim Dynasty](/wiki/Lore:Septim_Dynasty "Lore:Septim Dynasty") 200 years earlier, while others believe the empire is the only way Skyrim can survive and thus still worth preserving. A prophecy foretold by the [Elder Scrolls](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Scrolls "Lore:Elder Scrolls") is fully realized by this last event; [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") have returned to the land, and the Nordic god [Alduin](/wiki/Lore:Alduin "Lore:Alduin") rises to consume the world. The player character is the last [Dovahkiin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin") (or "dragonborn"), a mortal born with the soul of a dragon and able to speak their language. This prophecy is also spelled out on [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/File:SR-prerelease-Stone_Wall.jpg "File:SR-prerelease-Stone Wall.jpg"), a stone wall at [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"), the secret hidden refuge of the last of the Blades.[[3]](#cite_note-3)

## Gameplay

New gameplay features introduced include dual-wielding (assigning a weapon or spell to each hand, putting a spell in both hands makes an enhanced version of the spell), and new weapons that can be [smithed at a forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") from crafting materials. Unique finishing attacks are used for each weapon. Players can challenge (and be challenged by) certain NPCs to hand-to-hand brawls. Stamina can be expended quickly by choosing to "sprint", and backward movement is slower than forward movement.[[1]](#cite_note-FebGI-1)[[4]](#cite_note-VG247-4)

Character development has been changed as well; "class" selection is no longer used, the number of ["attributes"](/wiki/Skyrim:Attributes "Skyrim:Attributes") has been reduced to three (health, magicka or stamina), and instead of the twenty-one skills in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")* (twenty-seven in *[Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind"))*, Skyrim features eighteen [skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills"). Removed skills with no singularly defined skill replacement include *Blade* (shifted to other combat skills), *Blunt* (also shifted to other combat skills), *Hand to Hand*, *Mysticism* (spells shifted to other magic skills), *Athletics*, *Acrobatics*, and *Mercantile* (merged with another skill). The eighteen skills are:

| [Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Overview "Skyrim:Magic Overview") | [Combat](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat "Skyrim:Combat") | [Stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") | [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") | [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") |
| [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") | [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") | [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") |
| [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") | [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") | [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") |
| [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") | [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") | [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") |
| [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") | [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") | [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") |
| [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") | [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") |

Character [levels](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveling "Skyrim:Leveling") are no longer gained after a specific number of skill increases; rather it varies according to the skill level attained. The higher the skill level attained, the more progress is awarded towards the next character level. Therefore, faster player leveling can be achieved by focusing on increasing developed skills. Additionally, the lack of a class system eliminates the distinction between Major and Minor skills present in previous games; all skills provide equal leveling progress and will increase at the same rates for all characters upon creation. However, activating a [Guardian Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones") will speed the increase of its governed skills or give you a special power[[5]](#cite_note-Xbox360a-5)[[6]](#cite_note-G4E3Demo-6) Gaining a level also grants the player level-specific skill abilities and an increase in the attribute of the player's choosing. Each skill has a perk tree; upon gaining a level a player also gains a single perk 'point'. The point may be used at the time of leveling, or saved until the player sees fit to use it. Leveling above level 50 happens at a much decreased rate. [Level-scaling](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveling#Effects_of_Leveling "Skyrim:Leveling") is used, but is more comparable to the system in *Fallout 3* than the one in *Oblivion*. There are ten playable [races](/wiki/Skyrim:Races "Skyrim:Races"), the player character is still very customizable, and beards and customizable body features are among the new options available.[[1]](#cite_note-FebGI-1)[[4]](#cite_note-VG247-4) The [Sneak icon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak#Skill_Usage "Skyrim:Sneak") appears as an eye symbol on the crosshair as in *Oblivion*, and now varies depending on NPCs' level of awareness as in *Fallout 3*. A slightly open eye means the enemy is alert and knows someone is hiding, a medium-open eye means the enemy is actively searching, and an open eye means the enemy has found the player. A single *Crafting* skill is associated with each of the three main skill groups: [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") for Magic, [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") for Combat, and [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") for Stealth.

In common with *Morrowind* and *Oblivion*, [Vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") is present in Skyrim, and it is possible for the player to become infected and turn into a vampire.[[7]](#cite_note-7) Players can also contract [Lycanthropy](/wiki/Lore:Lycanthropy "Lore:Lycanthropy") and turn into [Werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf").

The main quest takes approximately 30 hours to complete in addition to the hundreds of hours of side quests to be completed.[[8]](#cite_note-PCGamer30-8)

## NPCs

Player/NPC interactions have been improved. Conversations between the player and NPCs do not freeze the rest of the game world, and the NPCs continue their activities while occasionally glancing at the player. A new system has been developed for quests, known as the [Radiant System](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"). NPCs react to the player's actions in new ways, such as fighting over possession of an item dropped by the player or attempting to return it to the player. The shop of a killed NPC may be inherited by another NPC, who may then offer the items/quests of the first. The player may also [marry an NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") of either gender,[[9]](#cite_note-9) and if they own a house, their spouse can live in it with them.[[10]](#cite_note-10) The player's actions also directly affect side quest creation, as well as altering parts of quests. NPCs can now be seen visibly performing tasks suited to their roles (e.g. a cook will be cooking) unlike previous games where they just stood still.

The faces of NPCs have been extensively overhauled and show distinct differences between races and more varied emotional expressions.[[1]](#cite_note-FebGI-1)[[4]](#cite_note-VG247-4) A large set of example character images was posted on Bethesda's Blog on August 24. The images can be found [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Pre-Release_Content#August_24_Race_Screenshots "Skyrim:Pre-Release Content").

### Voice Acting

NPCs are voiced by a cast of [more than 70 actors](/wiki/Skyrim:Voice_Actors "Skyrim:Voice Actors"). [Christopher Plummer](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0001626/ "imdbname:0001626") plays [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir"), a powerful [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") elder; [Max Von Sydow](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0001884/ "imdbname:0001884") plays [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern"), a chronicler and agent of the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") who has survived in hiding; [Joan Allen](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0000260/ "imdbname:0000260") is [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine"), one of the last remaining members of the Blades, and [Lynda Carter](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0004812/ "imdbname:0004812") returns as a Nord hero named [Gormlaith Golden-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Gormlaith_Golden-Hilt "Skyrim:Gormlaith Golden-Hilt"). The game also features [Michael Hogan](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0389581/ "imdbname:0389581") as [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius"), [Vladimir Kulich](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0474520/ "imdbname:0474520") as Nordic Jarl [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), and [Claudia Christian](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0160004/ "imdbname:0160004") as Tullius's chief lieutenant, [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke"). Other voice actors include [Diane Louise Salinger](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0758405/ "imdbname:0758405"), [Renee Victor](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0896149/ "imdbname:0896149") and [George Coe](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0168642/ "imdbname:0168642").[[11]](#cite_note-11)

## World

Click [here](/wiki/File:SR-prerelease-Stone_Wall.jpg "File:SR-prerelease-Stone Wall.jpg") for the full image of Alduin's Wall, featured in the teaser trailer.

Five large cities, comparatively larger than those in *Oblivion*, are available to explore (and to be attacked from above by dragons), along with a wider variety of caves and subterranean areas. The main five cities are walled and located in separate worlds to conserve memory (like *Oblivion*) but the 4 minor cities and 7 towns will be open (like *Morrowind*). Fast-traveling to locations already discovered has returned. Cooking, farming, wood-cutting, and mining, in addition to weapon-smithing, can be done in different towns. Children are also featured in the game.[[1]](#cite_note-FebGI-1)[[4]](#cite_note-VG247-4)

New factions include the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") (mercenary guild), the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") (mages guild), and the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") (rebellion).[[12]](#cite_note-12)
The [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") and the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") and [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") return as joinable factions.

The 150+ dungeons in the game were created by a team of eight, whereas *Oblivion'*s dungeons were all created by one designer.[[13]](#cite_note-Gamestooge130-13)

Upon a giant mountain, the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Lore:Throat_of_the_World "Lore:Throat of the World") houses the home of the [Greybeards](/wiki/Lore:Greybeards "Lore:Greybeards"), [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Lore:High_Hrothgar "Lore:High Hrothgar"), at the head of 7,000 steps.[[14]](#cite_note-14)

Skyrim features horses as mounts. Hostile creatures include: spiders, trolls, ice wraiths, zombies, sabre-toothed cats, wolves, daedra, skeletons, draugr and dragons.[[1]](#cite_note-FebGI-1)[[4]](#cite_note-VG247-4)

Some creatures such as mammoths and giants are non-hostile until the player moves too close to them.[[6]](#cite_note-G4E3Demo-6)

"Dynamic shadows" are used and snow falls and accumulates dynamically. Plants move more believably with the wind, and the water in the game actually flows along a course.[[1]](#cite_note-FebGI-1)[[4]](#cite_note-VG247-4)

## Items

Skyrim, like its predecessors, features a wide variety of weapons and armor of varying materials and quality, as well as many unique weapons, armor pieces, and tools to discover.

Weapons and armor no longer degrade with use.[[15]](#cite_note-15) Instead, the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") skill is used to craft new equipment and improve weapons and armor using raw materials from the new mining and leather working activities. Nearly any piece of equipment (even powerful Daedric artifacts) can be enhanced, and a skilled smith can vastly improve the quality of their gear.

[Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") allows the player to further enhance their items with magic. Enchanters can expend a [Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") to add magical effects to any weapon, armor, clothing, or jewelry that does not already contain an enchantment. New enchanting effects can be learned by disenchanting magic items found in the world.

The inventory menu now includes a preview with the ability to rotate and view any item you are carrying. This can be used to admire your gear and see what an item looks like without the need to drop it into the world, and some objects must be closely examined this way for clues on how to proceed in certain quests.[[16]](#cite_note-Footage20mins-16)

## Music

The game's soundtrack has been composed by [Jeremy Soule](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jeremy_Soule "wikipedia:Jeremy Soule"), who was also responsible for the music in [Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Music "Morrowind:Music") and [Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Music "Oblivion:Music"). Although much of the music is new, at least one track featured in preview videos has appeared before: the track at the start of [this](http://www.youtube.com/watch?feature=player_embedded&v=Kt7IeycKJKQ#!) demo is known as *Rise to Reality* or *Silt Sunrise* in Morrowind, and *Through the Valleys* in Oblivion. The soundtrack is being released as a four-disc set through [DirectSong](http://www.directsong.com/mobile/productdetails.php?productid=2240).[[17]](#cite_note-17)

## Development and Release

The name for the fifth main installment of the series was originally planned to be named [Romanelli](/wiki/Redguard:Easter_Eggs#Future_Games "Redguard:Easter Eggs") in 1998, before eventually being re-titled to Skyrim.

The game was released on November 11, 2011, worldwide on the Xbox 360, PS3, and PC platforms rated as M for mature,[[18]](#cite_note-18) and could be pre-ordered from several online retailers, such as [GameStop](http://www.gamestop.com/browse/search.aspx?dsNav=Ntk:TitleKeyword%7CElder+Scrolls+V%3a+Skyrim%7C1%7C) and [Amazon](http://www.amazon.com/s/ref=nb_sb_noss?url=search-alias%3Dvideogames&field-keywords=Elder+Scrolls+V%3A+Skyrim&rh=n%3A468642%2Ck%3AElder+Scrolls+V%3A+Skyrim&ajr=3). It uses an all-new graphics/gameplay engine called the "Creation Engine"[[19]](#cite_note-19) that uses some of the elements from *Oblivion* and *Fallout 3/New Vegas*, but new talent was also brought in to improve on the characters and animation of previous Bethesda titles.[[20]](#cite_note-20)

The game editor, previously called the Construction Set and now known as the Creation Kit, works in a similar way to previous versions.[[21]](#cite_note-21)

It was confirmed that the game will be integrated with the Steamworks distribution system.[[22]](#cite_note-22)

The game is rated M (Mature) in North America,[[23]](#cite_note-23) but is provisionally rated 15 in the UK [[24]](#cite_note-24) and MA15+ in Australia.

The minimum PC specification is Win XP/7/Vista (32 or 64 bit), dual core 2GHz CPU, 2GB RAM, DirectX 9c video card with 512MB RAM, plus Internet Access for Steam activation. The recommended specification is Win XP/7, quad-core CPU, 4GB RAM, 6GB HD, DirectX compatible sound card, DirectX 9 video card with 1 GB RAM - a GTX 260/Radeon 4890 or higher. According to Bethesda VP Pete Hines, *"The Min specs get you playing,. The recommended specs let you play on High, not on Ultra. You'll want beefier rig for that."* [[25]](#cite_note-25)

### Downloadable Content

There are several pieces of downloadable content ([DLC](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons")). The first two major DLCs were commissioned to be exclusive to the Xbox 360 for 30 days, after which they were made available for the PC.[[26]](#cite_note-26) Due to issues with the performance of the PS3, none of the content released in 2012 was made available for download until February of the following year.[[27]](#cite_note-27)

### Skyrim: Special Edition

At E3 2016, Bethesda announced ***Skyrim: [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition")***, a remaster of *Skyrim* for PlayStation 4, Xbox One, and PC. The rerelease contains "the game and add-ons with all-new features like remastered art and effects, volumetric god rays, dynamic depth of field, screen-space reflections and more". As with *Fallout 4*, it allows users of the console versions of the game to download mods. It was free on release to anyone who owned the base game and all DLC on Steam. It was released on October 28, 2016. [[28]](#cite_note-28)

# Skyrim:Achievements

## Overview

**Achievements** (specifically **[Xbox 360](/wiki/Skyrim:Xbox_360 "Skyrim:Xbox 360") Achievements**, **Steam Achievements**, and **[PlayStation 3](/wiki/Skyrim:PlayStation_3 "Skyrim:PlayStation 3") Trophies**) are awards given to the player for accomplishing various milestones in the game. Fifty achievements and fifty-one trophies are available in the basic game. [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") adds five achievements and [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add ten achievements each.

On the Xbox 360, a total of one thousand Gamer Points are available in the base game, or 1,550 points with all add-ons installed; the "Points" column in the following table provides the Gamer Points associated with each specific achievement. On the PC, Steam achievements stand on their own and don't include points. In addition, use of [console commands](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and [mods](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Mods "Skyrim Mod:Mods") on the PC version does not prevent the awarding of achievements. On the PS3, the Trophies are sorted into types: Bronze, Silver and Gold. Earning every trophy from the base game will unlock [a Platinum trophy](#Platinum_Trophy).

The [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition") has a separate achievement list for Steam, Xbox One, and PS4, meaning they can be earned twice by playing both versions of the game. Note that the use of mods (including [Verified Creations](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Verified_Creations "Skyrim Mod:Verified Creations")) disables Special Edition achievement progress for both PC and console. Since the Special Edition comes with all three major add-ons, the achievement list contains all of the below add-on-related achievements by default (i.e. 75 achievements or 76 trophies). The use of [Creation Club Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") does not disable achievements as they are official content, however the Creation Club content does not add any additional achievements.

Similar to the Special Edition, [Skyrim VR](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_VR "Skyrim:Skyrim VR") also has a separate achievement list for Steam and PS4. The use of mods disables achievement progress on PC.

More detailed information on how to unlock each achievement can be obtained by clicking on the achievement's name.

| [SR-achievement-Hidden Knowledge.png](/wiki/File:SR-achievement-Hidden_Knowledge.png) | 40 | Bronze | [Hidden Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Hidden_Knowledge "Skyrim:Hidden Knowledge") | Learn the secrets of 5 [Black Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)") |
| [SR-achievement-Stalhrim Crafter.png](/wiki/File:SR-achievement-Stalhrim_Crafter.png) | 20 | Silver | [Stalhrim Crafter](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Crafter "Skyrim:Stalhrim Crafter") | Craft an item out of [Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") |
| [SR-achievement-Dragonrider.png](/wiki/File:SR-achievement-Dragonrider.png) | 20 | Bronze | [Dragonrider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrider "Skyrim:Dragonrider") | Tame and ride 5 [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") |
| [SR-achievement-Raven Rock Owner.png](/wiki/File:SR-achievement-Raven_Rock_Owner.png) | 20 | Bronze | [Raven Rock Owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Owner "Skyrim:Raven Rock Owner") | Own a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Severin_Manor "Skyrim:Severin Manor") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") |
| [SR-achievement-Solstheim Explorer.png](/wiki/File:SR-achievement-Solstheim_Explorer.png) | 30 | Bronze | [Solstheim Explorer](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim_Explorer "Skyrim:Solstheim Explorer") | Discover 30 locations on the island of Solstheim |

## Missable Achievements

Most of the achievements can be obtained regardless of your previous game choices. However, a handful of achievements can be missed:

-  **[Oblivion Walker](/wiki/Skyrim:Oblivion_Walker "Skyrim:Oblivion Walker")** (30 pts/Silver) — Collect 15 Daedric [Artifacts](/wiki/Skyrim:Artifacts "Skyrim:Artifacts")
  - There are a total of sixteen available Daedric Artifacts that qualify for this achievement, five of which can be missed depending upon your choices during each associated [Daedric Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Quests "Skyrim:Daedric Quests"). See [Oblivion Walker](/wiki/Skyrim:Oblivion_Walker "Skyrim:Oblivion Walker") for more details.
-  **[One with the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:One_with_the_Shadows "Skyrim:One with the Shadows")** (30 pts/Silver) — Returned the Thieves Guild to its former glory
  - Can be missed if Erikur dies before completing The Dainty Sload. After starting Bound Until Death, he is no longer essential and can be killed.
-  **[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These...#Achievements "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")** (10 pts/Bronze) — Join the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood")
-  **[Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death#Achievements "Skyrim:Bound Until Death")** (10 pts/Bronze) — Complete Bound Until Death
-  **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis!#Achievements "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")** (30 pts/Silver) — Complete Hail Sithis!
  - All three Dark Brotherhood achievements become unavailable if you choose to [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")
-  **[War Hero](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Hero "Skyrim:War Hero")** (10 pts/Bronze) — Capture [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") or [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall")
  - The associated quest ([The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)") or [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)")) can be skipped depending upon the outcome of [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending").
-  **[Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow_(achievement) "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow (achievement)")** (20 pts/Bronze) — Use the special power of [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow")
  - [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow") is not marked as a quest item after completing [Kindred Judgement](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgement "Skyrim:Kindred Judgement"), so this achievement can be missed if the bow is lost or despawns.
-  **[Werewolf Mastered](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf_Mastered "Skyrim:Werewolf Mastered")** (20 pts/Bronze) — Acquire 11 [werewolf perks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy#Skill_Perks "Skyrim:Lycanthropy")
  - After curing lycanthropy twice (either using a [Glenmoril Witch Head](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch_Head "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch Head") or by becoming a [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord")), the player will never be able to become a werewolf or acquire werewolf perks again.
-  **[Stalhrim Crafter](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Crafter "Skyrim:Stalhrim Crafter")** (20 pts/Silver) — Craft an item out of [Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim")
  - The associated quest can be missed if [Deor Woodcutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter") or [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice") dies before it starts.

## Notes

-  Achievements are absent from the [Nintendo Switch version](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch") of the game.

## Bugs

-  Achievements can occasionally be missed by Steam and PS4, even though they have been completed in-game.
  - To fix this, reload an earlier save and re-complete the achievement.
  - Making sure that the "Enable the Steam Overlay while in-game" is enabled (from the Steam client's properties) before starting the game prevents this issue.

Acolyte Aldren

**Acolyte Aldren** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [acolyte](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerRestorationMaster "Skyrim:TrainerRestorationMaster") of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth"). She can send you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_from_the_Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Note from the Temple of Kynareth") during [A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish") requesting [Ironwood Soup](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironwood_Soup "Skyrim:Ironwood Soup") in order to heal [Rulnik Wind-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Rulnik_Wind-Strider "Skyrim:Rulnik Wind-Strider") from ataxia.

## Related Quests

- **[A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Make a bitter choice.

### A Dying Wish

Acolyte Aldren and Rulnik

:   **I have the Ironwood Soup you're looking for.**
:   *"You've done well."*

:   :   **Here you are.**
    :   *"Thank you."*

:   :   **I'll give it to you, but not for free.**
    :   *"Okay. Just this once."*

Acolyte Jenssen

**Acolyte Jenssen** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") at the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

Jenssen spends his entire life inside the temple, tending to the sick and injured by using his [restore health](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health") and [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Stamina "Skyrim:Restore Stamina") spells to effectively cure them. From midnight to 8am he sleeps in one of the available beds. If Whiterun is attacked as part of the civil war, Jenssen will make an exception and help repair the temple walls, going outside at 1pm and spend three hours using his hammer on the wall near the entrance.

He wears a set of [monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Monk Robes") with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Boots"), and carries the [key to Wintersand Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Wintersand_Manor "Skyrim:Key to Wintersand Manor") along with a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). He doesn't wield any weapons and instead relies on a selection of spells, specifically [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing"), [Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks"), [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt") and [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh").

## Dialogue

While healing his patients, he will check in on their condition regularly, asking:

:   *"How are you feeling?"*
:   *"How do you feel?"*
:   *"Feeling any better?"*

He might ask the [wounded soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Wounded_Soldier "Skyrim:Wounded Soldier") specifically:

:   *"How is the pain? Any better?"*

And the [sickly farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Sickly_Farmer "Skyrim:Sickly Farmer"):

:   *"Has your fever cooled?"*

He will also reassure them from time to time, saying comforting things such as:

:   *"Patience. The body needs time to mend."*
:   *"More rest will do you good."*
:   *"Try to relax. You'll be well soon enough."*

He shares these lines with his fellow healers, [Ahlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahlam "Skyrim:Ahlam") and [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

## Notes

- His colleague Ahlam and her husband [Nazeem](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazeem "Skyrim:Nazeem") were originally meant to live inside their own house, Wintersand Manor. Both of them still carry the key to this nonexistent house, but Jenssen does so as well, although it's unknown as to why exactly this is. He might have been meant to visit there, but it might have also been added to his inventory on mistake. While Nazeem and Ahlam are also part of the house's relevant ownership faction, Jenssen is not.

## Bugs

- He carries the key to Wintersand Manor, but there is no such place to be found in Skyrim.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Activities

## Overview

A range of **activities** are possible in Skyrim. Some are obvious parts of gameplay, such as completing [quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Quests "Skyrim:Quests") and exploring [dungeons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons"). This page lists some of the optional activities that are available.

## Crafting

You are able to make a range of custom items, using the various crafting [skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills"), specifically:

- [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"): Create potions by using two or more ingredients with the same effect. You can also try to discover new effects by combining random ingredients, though this may fail to produce anything.
- [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting"): Enchant weapons or apparel with magical properties.
  - [Staff Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Enchant magical staffs with the spells you know.
- [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"): Create and improve weapons and apparel.
  - [Forges](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), [grindstones](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), [workbenches](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") and [anvils](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") are used for the various smithing activities

Other types of crafting are not controlled by any skills:

- [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge"): Create staves, spell scrolls, spell tomes and Daedric items.
- [Baking](/wiki/Skyrim:Baking "Skyrim:Baking")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Baked food is more nutritious than raw food.
- [Bone Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Forge "Skyrim:Bone Forge")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Hall "Skyrim:Gallows Hall"): Summon permanently bound undead followers.
- [Construction](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Build your own house from raw materials.
- [Cooking](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking"): Cooked food is more nutritious than raw food.
- [Imbuing Chamber](/wiki/Skyrim:Imbuing_Chamber "Skyrim:Imbuing Chamber")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Create dangerous [magical spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Scrolls "Skyrim:Spider Scrolls") for use as weapons.
- [Mining](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining"): Mine ore for use in smithing or to sell.
- [Smelting](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelting "Skyrim:Smelting"): Mineral ores need to be smelted before they can be used at weapon forging.
- [Tanning](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"): Convert hides into leather and leather into leather strips.

### Quests

- **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Other Tasks

- **[Cutting Lumber](/wiki/Skyrim:Cutting_Lumber "Skyrim:Cutting Lumber")**: Serves no purpose except for roleplaying in the original version of the game. If [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed, sawn logs can be cut at wood mills, with the permission of the mill owner.
- **[Milling](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling")**: Serves no purpose except for roleplaying in the original version of the game. If Hearthfire is installed, [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") can be used to create [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour").
- **[Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity) "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Pick up a [fishing rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Rod") and reel in rare fish and other items.

## Life

- [Adoption](/wiki/Skyrim:Child#Adoption "Skyrim:Child")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")
- [Houses](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses")
- [Marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage")
- [Sleeping](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping "Skyrim:Sleeping")
- [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane")

## Interactions

- [Brawls](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl")
- [Hide and Seek](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_and_Seek_(game) "Skyrim:Hide and Seek (game)")
- [Tag, you're it!](/wiki/Skyrim:Tag,_you%27re_it! "Skyrim:Tag, you're it!")
- [World Interactions](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions")

## Achievements

[Achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") related to activities are:

-  **[Architect](/wiki/Skyrim:Architect "Skyrim:Architect")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") (10 points/Bronze) — Build three wings on a house
-  **[Artificer](/wiki/Skyrim:Artificer "Skyrim:Artificer")** (10 points/Bronze) — Make a [smithed](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") item, an [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") item, and a [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy")
  - Note that [cooking](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") counts as making a potion for this achievement.
-  **[Citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen "Skyrim:Citizen")** (10 points/Bronze) — Buy a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses")
-  **[Hard Worker](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Worker "Skyrim:Hard Worker")** (10 points/Bronze) — [Chop wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood"), [mine ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining"), and [cook food](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking")
-  **[Land Baron](/wiki/Skyrim:Land_Baron "Skyrim:Land Baron")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") (10 points/Bronze) — Buy three plots of land
-  **[Landowner](/wiki/Skyrim:Landowner "Skyrim:Landowner")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") (10 points/Bronze) — Buy a plot of land
-  **[Married](/wiki/Skyrim:Married "Skyrim:Married")** (10 points/Bronze) — Get [married](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage")
-  **[Proud Parent](/wiki/Skyrim:Proud_Parent "Skyrim:Proud Parent")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") (10 points/Bronze) — Adopt a [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child")
-  **[Master Architect](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Architect "Skyrim:Master Architect")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") (10 points/Bronze) — Build three houses
  - Note that you must construct all three wings on each of the three houses to get credit for this achievement.

| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 80 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionReach](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach "Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach"); [Jeweler](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweler "Skyrim:Jeweler"); [MarkarthEndonsHouseFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthEndonsHouseFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthEndonsHouseFaction"); [TownMarkarthFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction "Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction") | | |

Adara

**Adara** is the [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [daughter](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") of [Kerah](/wiki/Skyrim:Kerah "Skyrim:Kerah") and [Endon](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon"), who are silversmiths in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). Her brother is Cade, who is off fighting with the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). When she grows up, she wants to be a silversmith like her parents; for now, she is apprenticed to her father. If anything befalls her mother, she technically takes over running Kerah's jewelry stall as well, standing behind it during business hours and attempting to attract customers. However, she does not offer you any merchant dialogue, making it impossible to trade with her. Her father is essential, so she cannot become an orphan.

She wakes at 8am and goes outside with her father, following him around. They can be found wandering the streets of Markarth until 8pm, when they and Kerah head to [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") to dine for three hours and [converse](#Conversations) with each other. They return home at 11pm, when Adara goes to bed.

Adara wears [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Shoes"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Endon%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Endon's House") to the [family's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon%27s_House "Skyrim:Endon's House"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Kerah%27s_Key "Skyrim:Kerah's Key") to her mother's jewelry case, a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

If you talk to Adara's father, Endon, he may mention her: *"My daughter Adara is also my apprentice. She's a quick study."* Kerah may also do the same: *"My daughter Adara is going to be a fine silversmith when she's older."* When conversing, Endon can be found praising their daughter, telling Kerah, *"Adara bends the silver so naturally. Grandmother would have cried if she saw how deft our daughter has become."* and *"Yes, I have. Adara made the rings herself. She is learning to bend the metal well."*

## Dialogue

When spoken to:

:   *"I'm going to be a silversmith one day, like my mother and father."*
:   *"Being an apprentice is great. I get to swing a hammer at things."*
:   *"Mama doesn't like me jumping up and down in the house, but I can't help it. I swear."*

When she is running Kerah's stall, she can be heard saying things like:

:   *"Jewelry for sale. Redguard craftsmanship in every piece."*
:   *"You there, uh, the finest silver in Markarth is sold right here."*
:   *"Maybe you could buy a gift for a friend? A best friend?"*

## Conversations

Adara can be seen chatting with her family at Silver-Blood Inn:

**Kerah**: *"What should we have tonight?"*
**Endon**: *"Something simple, a stew perhaps."*
**Adara**: *"Stew again, papa? I want steak."*
**Kerah**: *"Maybe we could spend a little bit more and buy some meat, Endon."*
**Endon**: *"May be. Let me think about it."*

At home, she may have more conversations:

**Adara**: *"Mama, when is Cade coming home?"*
**Kerah**: *"He's off fighting, Adara, with the Stormcloaks. He'll return when the war is over."*
**Endon**: *"Our son joining the Stormcloaks. If this war had never happened, Cade would have joined the Imperial Legion, like grandfather."*
**Kerah**: *"Endon, we talked about this... Are you still disappointed in Cade's choice?"*
**Endon**: *"No. I think if I was a young man, I would have done the same."*
**Adara**: *"Can I join the Legion when I grow up?"*
**Endon**: *"If there's still a Legion left, Adara. I'm sure you'd make a great soldier. Just like your brother."*

**Kerah**: *"We sold all those lovely little necklaces you brought me today. Did you make them yourself?"*
**Adara**: *"That's right! Papa helped me with the clasps, but I did all the links on my own."*
**Endon**: *"Adara bends the silver so naturally. Grandmother would have cried if she saw how deft our daughter has become."*
**Kerah**: *"Well, I'm proud of both of you. I haven't been so busy since those nobles from [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") come into the city three years ago."*
**Endon**: *"I miss those days, before the Forsworn took up arms again, when you could walk the roads in peace."*
**Kerah**: *"Endon, dear, please don't.... Save your frustrations for work."*
**Endon**: *"You're right, dear. I'm sorry to worry you."*

## Notes

- Although Adara says thinks like "jewelry for sale" when at her mother's stall, you cannot buy them from Adara directly.

## Bugs

- Adara doesn't own the bed assigned to her so she just sandboxes near it all night.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, addresses this issue. Her bed was also the wrong size.

# Skyrim:Add-ons

## Overview

This is a list of the **official add-ons**, downloadable content created or officially endorsed by [Bethesda Softworks](/wiki/General:Bethesda "General:Bethesda") for *[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")*. Five add-ons have been released for *Skyrim*, including two free add-ons exclusive to the PC version of the game. The [Creation Club](#Creation_Club) provides additional official content created by both Bethesda and external developers for the game's [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition"). The [Nintendo Switch](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch") version of the game features exclusive content that is unlocked in-game through the use of [amiibo](#Amiibo).

*[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")*, *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")*, and *[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")* are included as part of the [Legendary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Legendary_Edition "Skyrim:Legendary Edition") and the Special Edition. Neither of the free add-ons, [Fall of the Space Core, Vol 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_of_the_Space_Core,_Vol_1 "Skyrim:Fall of the Space Core, Vol 1") and the [High Resolution Texture Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Resolution_Texture_Pack "Skyrim:High Resolution Texture Pack"), are available for the Special Edition. The latter add-on is made redundant for this release, however, as the Special Edition uses high-resolution textures in place of the original assets. The [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") includes *Dawnguard*, *Hearthfire*, and *Dragonborn* and all [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") content.

## Creation Club

**[Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")** was an in-game [microtransactional](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microtransaction "wikipedia:Microtransaction") store for [Skyrim Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition"). A [virtual currency](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_goods "wikipedia:Virtual goods") called **Creation Club Credits** was sold within it, which was used to purchase unique add-ons called [Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creations "Skyrim:Creations"). Each Creation released through Creation Club is official [Bethesda](/wiki/General:Bethesda "General:Bethesda") content, developed with third-party developers and contracted [mod](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Mods "Skyrim Mod:Mods") authors. As official content, Creation Club content does not disable [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") acquisition.

The service entered beta on September 28, 2017 and officially launched on October 4, 2017. It was never available for [Skyrim VR](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_VR "Skyrim:Skyrim VR").

All 74 Creations are included in the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"). Special Edition and [Switch](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch") users also receive free access to four Creations: [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"), [Rare Curios](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Curios "Skyrim:Rare Curios"), [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), and [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"). Several other discounted Creations were offered for free either on a permanent or temporary basis. On Switch, the Anniversary Upgrade with all the Creations is available, but not the Creation Club itself.

As of December 5, 2023, Creation Club has been retired and the Verified Creator Program is intended to be its replacement. While Creation Club Creations are considered official content, [Verified Creator Program](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Verified_Creator_Program "Skyrim Mod:Verified Creator Program") Creations are considered third party [mods](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Mods "Skyrim Mod:Mods").

Addict

The **Addict** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") found dead in [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den") in one of the booths set up for enjoying [Redwater skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Skooma "Skyrim:Redwater Skooma"). She wears a [roughspun tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Roughspun_Tunic "Skyrim:Roughspun Tunic") and [footwraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Footwraps "Skyrim:Footwraps").

# Skyrim:Addvar's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

Addvar's House

**Addvar's House** is a small house in the residential district of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), next to [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House").

It is the home of town fishmonger [Addvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar "Skyrim:Addvar"), his wife [Greta](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta"), and their daughter [Svari](/wiki/Skyrim:Svari "Skyrim:Svari").

It contains only one zone, *[Addvar's House](#Walkthrough)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Addvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar "Skyrim:Addvar")  [Greta](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta")  [Svari](/wiki/Skyrim:Svari "Skyrim:Svari") |

## Related Quests

- **[Return to Grace](/wiki/Skyrim:Return_to_Grace "Skyrim:Return to Grace")**: Convince a mourning [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta") to go to the [local temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines").

## Walkthrough

Addvar's House interior

This house is a comfortably lit wooden building. To the left of the rug by the entrance is a basket holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), along with a small crate containing a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), and a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), as well as a nearby bucket holding a whole [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Hanging above the half-wall to the left are three rings, which hold a total of six [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and one [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)").

In the central area, there is a table with two chairs, above which are three hanging [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids. On the table are two tankards, a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), garlic, an [Eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and two identical meals on wooden plates, which consist of four [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") and [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"). In front of the fireplace is a [cooking](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") pot and a cast iron pot holding a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Mounted above the fireplace is a goat head.

To the left is a small area set aside for food preparation. Beneath an elk head mounted on the wall is a table with four tankards, a barrel of mead, a horn candle, two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), [beef stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Beef_Stew "Skyrim:Beef Stew"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), two and a half loaves of bread, two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), four grilled leeks, a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), seared slaughterfish, and a number of cheese wheels and wedges.

To the right are two rooms. The one next to the basket of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") contains a bed belonging to Svari. In this room are two respawning food barrels, a basket, a bucket, a non-respawning wardrobe, and a non-respawning end table with [Alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a horn candle on it. The next room is the pantry, with seven [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), seven [Eidar cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), six potatoes, three cabbages, and two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). On top of one shelving unit is a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), and on the other is a copy of the book *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")*. There are also three respawning food barrels stacked behind the shelving units, and a few clutter items. Next to this room, under the stairs, is a non-respawning chest containing a small amount of gold, with a high chance for an [animal part](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Parts "Skyrim:Animal Parts") or other miscellaneous item to appear, and a very small chance of a torch appearing.

The upper level has a number of small items, along with a few pieces of furniture to sit on. On a long crate there rests a non-respawning large sack and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). The nearby chest (non-respawning) only has loot if you have [Imperial Luck](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Luck "Skyrim:Imperial Luck"), [Prowler's Profit](/wiki/Skyrim:Prowler%27s_Profit "Skyrim:Prowler's Profit"), or [Golden Touch](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Touch_(perk) "Skyrim:Golden Touch (perk)"). On the adjacent cupboard (non-respawning) are a gourd, a gold piece, [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#000cee80 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"), a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), three pieces of garlic, some tundra cotton, a clothes iron, and a human skull. On a thin table near this cupboard are an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a roll of paper, a tankard, and a horn candle. In a corner is a double bed belonging to Addvar. Near this bed are a non-respawning end table and a table with a chair next to it. On the table are two tankards, some bread, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a melted candle.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Addvar's House") to which is carried by Greta and Svari.
- There is a "Loot" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the bottom left of the entrance door.

## Bugs

- The double bed is only owned by Addvar, which results in Greta being unable to use it, and therefore she isn't able to sleep at all.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.4, fixes this bug.

Addvar selling fish at his stand in Solitude

**Addvar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") fishmonger selling his wares from the market in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). He is the husband of [Greta](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta") and father of [Svari](/wiki/Skyrim:Svari "Skyrim:Svari"). His wife will take over running their marketplace stall if he dies.

While his wife lost all hope following the execution of her brother [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir"), Addvar seems focused on providing his family a proper income during tough times. He gets out of bed at 6am and heads to the market, where he sells his produce for a whopping fourteen hours in a row. At 8pm he returns to [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") and spends the evening enjoying the cooking of his wife and the company of his daughter. At midnight, he heads upstairs and goes to bed. While he will promote his services around the clock, you can only trade with him from his stall.

Like the rest of his family, Addvar is quite poor and his attire reflects that. He wears a set of cheap merchant's [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"). Due to a bug he doesn't carry his house key, but a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Cage_Key "Skyrim:Cage Key") to one of the prison cells in [the Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire"). He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

At all times, Addvar will promote his fish business around the clock, saying:

:   *"Plenty of fresh fish for ya."*
:   *"I've got some salmon to sell."*
:   *"You shouldn't leave Solitude without trying our fish. Best in Skyrim."*
:   *"Fresh fish! Fresh fish!"*
:   *"Fresh Fish! Straight from the Fjords!"*
:   *"The finest fish, here! Caught daily!"*

When spoken to:

:   **Where do you catch the fish?**
:   *"Down at the docks. There are a few good spots, if you can avoid the East Empire Company workers and those Red Wave thugs."*

:   **You and your daughter were at the execution.**
:   *"Svari, yes. It's been hard on her. The girl misses her uncle. I've tried to explain that Roggvir did something bad and that we all have to be accountable for our actions but... a child feels what she will."*

Upon exiting conversation he can say:

:   *"These are troubled times. Be on your guard out there."*
:   *"May the gods speed your journeys... and steady your sword arm."*

## Conversations

Addvar tells Svari to go home

When you first arrive in Solitude, you will witness Roggvir being executed and Addvar mercifully asking his daughter to go home. [Vivienne Onis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis") will be present as well, and the following scene will play out:

**Svari:** *"They can't hurt uncle Roggvir. Tell them he didn't do it."*
**Addvar:** *"Svari, you need to go home. Go home and stay there until your mother comes."*
**Vivienne:** *"You should tell her that her uncle is scum that betrayed his High King. Best she know now, Addvar."*
**Addvar:** *"You're all heart, Vivienne."*

Also, if you visit Addvar's house in the evening, these conversations can be heard:

**Addvar:** *"Svari, Jala said you stole an apple from her cart yesterday. Is this true?"*
**Svari**: *"Just a little one! I was hungry!"*
**Greta**: *"I'll talk with Jala, dear. I'm sure she'll accept a potato as repayment."*
**Addvar**: *"I suppose. But Svari, we don't steal. We're better than that. Understand?"*
**Svari**: *"Yes, papa."*

**Greta**: *"Eat up, Svari."*
**Svari**: *"Fish? Again?"* or *"Potatoes? Again?"*
**Addvar**: *"It's all we've got for today. Don't be greedy."*
**Greta**: *"Maybe we'll have better luck tomorrow."*
**Addvar**: *"We'll make it, Greta. We always have so far..."*

## Notes

- While most merchants who deal in food (such as inn and barkeepers) have one or two seared slaughterfish for sale, Addvar can have upwards of 30 for sale at a time, as well as the same amount of salmon meat, or steaks.

## Bugs

- Addvar was accidentally given a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Cage_Key "Skyrim:Cage Key") to one of the cages in [Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire") instead of his regular [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Addvar's House").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- Considerable dialogue was written for Addvar and his various customers. Unfortunately, they were recorded in [Jala](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala "Skyrim:Jala")'s voice. Some are improbable for Jala, and conditions are set to prevent them. The rest are rarely heard, as they are mixed with Jala's other dialogue.

:   **Addvar**: *"A little late in the day for your rounds Sorex."*
:   **Sorex**: *"I seem to have more chores for the Winking Skeever each day. I still have a delivery to do too."*

:   **Silana**: *"Fresh fish sounds like just the thing today, Addvar."*
:   **Addvar**: *"I've been pushing the Salmon but I'll tell you the Slaughterfish is a bit better today."*
:   **Silana**: *"Thank you, Addvar, I am picky about what I eat these days."*

:   **Aia**: *"Salmon sounds good today."*
:   **Addvar**: *"Speaking of sounding good, I've heard a couple of your classmates on the street recently."*
:   **Aia**: *"As long as they're playing instruments they're passable. You don't want to hear them sing."*

:   **Rorlund**: *"I wish we could have absolved your brother-in-law of his sins before his execution."*
:   **Addvar**: *"I don't think he would have wanted your absolution, Rorlund. He worshiped Talos. I appreciate the thought though."*

:   **Addvar**: *"Jawanan, I don't see you here often."*
:   **Jawanan**: *"I do not like fish."*
:   **Addvar**: *"Okay. Well. That's all I've got."*
:   **Jawanan**: *"I am buying a fish for Noster. He likes fish."*
:   **Addvar**: *"A sale's a sale but I have to know... why are you buying something for Noster?"*
:   **Jawanan**: *"A war veteran should be respected."*

:   **Illdi**: *"I'm sorry about Roggvir. It's a shame, I liked him."*
:   **Addvar**: *"Greta is taking it hardest. She won't go to the Temple of Divines anymore."*

:   **Ataf**: *"I went out ice fishing a few days ago."*
:   **Addvar**: *"Brave man, with the Blackbloods out there. Did you catch anything?"*
:   **Ataf**: *"Naw, mostly just froze."*
:   **Addvar**: *"Well, keep at it. The fish have to get to know you before they're willing to bite."*

# Skyrim:Addvild

## Overview

Addvild working at Snow-Shod Farm

**Addvild** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") who works for [Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod") at [Snow-Shod Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Farm "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Farm") with his recently married wife, [Leonara Arius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leonara_Arius "Skyrim:Leonara Arius"). He [appreciates](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat") honest work and will pay a septim each for [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and five septims each for [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat").

He starts his day at 6am with a one-hour breakfast at the farmhouse. At 7am, he goes outside to tend the crops and look after the farm animals until his bedtime at midnight, taking a break at 7pm to dine at the house for one hour.

He wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#.28000209A6.29 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"). He wields a [leveled dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") in combat and carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") along with [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

Regarding his position, he is extremely appreciative of Vulwulf Snow-Shod for trusting him to take care of the farm without supervision. This is evident in his oft-repeated phrases:

:   *"Vulwulf has been quite generous to let me take care of their farm considering I am not part of their family."*
:   *"The Snow-Shod's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *are very trusting to let me run this place without their supervision."*

Also when spoken to:

:   *"I'm glad there are guards outside the farm. I don't think I could defend the place alone."*
:   *"If you're looking to purchase goods, I have none to sell. You should head into [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") instead."*
:   *"Pretty quiet out here on the farm. My wife and I kind of like the solitude."*

If you have cleared out [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth")'s safe during the quest [Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear") and have not returned to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"), Addvild will express concern about the nearby [estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate"):

:   *"Did you see the fires from Goldenglow Estate? I was afraid the whole place was going to burn to the ground!"*

## Conversations

He may converse with his Leonara:

:   **Leonara**: *"My darling, you've made me the happiest woman in all Skyrim."*
:   **Addvild**: *"It brings me joy to hear that, but what possessed you to say that so suddenly?"*
:   **Leonara**: *"I've already lost a family, and we're about to start a new one. I don't want that to happen again."*
:   **Addvild**: *"My sweet Leanora*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, I will never let anything happen to us. I promise."*

:   **Leonara**: *"I'm not so sure the few guards they've assigned to the farm are enough."*
:   **Addvild**: *"It will have to do. Besides, if it came to blows, I'm sure the Snow-Shod's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *would come out here and assist us."*
:   **Leonara**: *"I suppose so. I just fear they won't make it out here in time."*
:   **Addvild**: *"Just worry about keeping the fields tended and let the Jarl worry about the war."*

## Bugs

- Addvild's first greeting sounds *"Honest pay for honest work."*, but the text shows *"We could always use help picking crops if you need a few extra coins."*

Adeber

**Adeber** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who works at [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine"). He isn't really a talker because he is too busy digging out ore.

Adeber will spend all of his time working inside the mine, never taking a break to eat, sleep, or go outside. He wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries around a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Left_Hand_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Key to Left Hand Miner's Barracks") to [Left Hand Miner's Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Left Hand Miner's Barracks"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

Attempting to speak to Adeber will have him say:

:   *"I'm one of miners. Plenty of ore to dig up around here."*
:   *"Don't have much to say to you. Got work."*

Adelaisa Vendicci

Adelaisa in the office

**Adelaisa Vendicci** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who works for the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). She appears during [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East"), when she visits [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")'s [East Empire Company office](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_(place) "Skyrim:East Empire Company (place)") to check on its condition. She later boards a ship with you to assault the pirate gang [Blood Horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker"), and can be recruited as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") afterward.

Once the Blood Horkers have been taken care of, she will have a new responsibility to inspect the East Empire Company office. At 7am she walks down the streets of Windhelm for a breath of fresh air. She eats some breakfast at 8am before she returns to work at the office at 9am, staying there for ten hours. At 7pm she spends the evening dining at [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub"), though she was intended to go to [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") as well (see [bugs](#Bugs)). At midnight she goes back to the office, though she was supposed to sleep at this time.

Adelaisa Vendicci wears a set of [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"), [Imperial bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Bracers") and [Imperial boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Boots"). In combat she will rely on her [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"). She also carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), the [East Empire office key](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Office_Key "Skyrim:East Empire Office Key") and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").

### Rise in the East

Once you've gathered information surrounding the Blood Horkers, return to [Orthus Endario](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthus_Endario "Skyrim:Orthus Endario"), who is busy apologizing to Adelaisa for the sorry state of the office:

:   **Orthus**: *"Adelaisa, I'm sorry."*
:   **Adelaisa**: *"Sorry isn't good enough, Orthus. There's a lot of gold at stake here, and sniveling isn't going to get it back."*
:   **Orthus**: *"I've got a top man/woman on the job right now. He/She should be returning any moment."*
:   **Adelaisa**: *"This must be him/her, then."*

When spoken to after this conversation:

:   **I know where the Blood Horkers are.**
:   *"Finally, someone around here that can get things done. Since we're short on soldiers you'll be coming with us, too. No arguments.
    Anything else you want to say?"*
:   **Their leader is a battle-mage named Haldyn.**
:   *"Haldyn? I've heard of the man, but never guess he'd join up with some pirates. This could be even more dangerous than I thought. Head to the ships. We'll plan the assault on the way."*

Once she has addressed you, she will stay in the building until you board the ship to [Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly").

During the journey, the ship will come to a sudden stop, anchoring near an island covered with a strange fog. When you speak to her:

:   **What's the plan?**
:   *"Well, here we are. We think."*

    :   **Have we reached Japhet's Folly?**
    :   *"Hard to say. The weather's taken a bit of a turn, here. Haldyn's been known to obscure his hideaways with magic. If we take care of him, the way should be clear to properly assault the island."*

        :   **Is that my job?**
        :   *"You've shown yourself useful so far. All these lunks are too afraid of Haldyn to head in before the fog's cleared. So if you're willing to perform one more service for the Company, we could put this matter behind us for good. Take out Haldyn, and we'll handle the rest."*

Once Haldyn lies dead, return to Adelaisa, who is waiting at the docks. Upon greeting her, she will say:

:   *"There you are."*
:   **I've killed Haldyn.**
:   *"Impressive work. We started the attack once you made the fog scamper away like that. Hope you didn't catch any of the fire.
    We can head back whenever you're set. There's celebrating to be done! Are you ready to go?"*

:   :   **Let's go.**

        :   *"All aboard!"*

:   :   **Not just yet.**

        :   *"Let me know. We shouldn't stay here all day. My men want their mead."*

## Dialogue

When spoken to after Rise in the East is complete:

:   *"We can't thank you enough for helping us get this office running."*
:   *"I appreciate everything you've done for us, but I really am quite busy."*
:   *"Glad Orthus was able to find someone competent to help out."*
:   *"You handled yourself pretty well back at Japhet's Folly. We'll remember that."*
:   *"Hey, it's our hero! Seen any more of those pirates around here?"*

## Notes

- Adelaisa is of the very few characters in the game who uses Imperial armor and an Imperial sword who isn't a member of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- Although her default gear is governed by the Heavy Armor skill, Adelaisa is actually more proficient in Light Armor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. It changes her class to [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H").

## Bugs

- Adelaisa's schedule seems to have discrepancies: her package name indicates that she should sleep from midnight to 7am, but there is nowhere to sleep in the office.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0, fixes this bug.
- On [Morndas](/wiki/Lore:Calendar "Lore:Calendar"), Middas, and Fredas, she was also supposed to dine at New Gnisis Cornerclub from 7pm to midnight, while on other days she chooses [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"), but the schedule always points to the Cornerclub.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Adisla

## Overview

| Adisla (RefID: 00029970) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | | |
| House | [Hlaalu Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00029970 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001411E |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 75 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 60 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 60 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleCommoner](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionEastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch"); [Hlaalu Farm Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm_Faction "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm Faction") | | |

Adisla tending to her crops at [Hlaalu Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm")

**Adisla** is an aging [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") working the land for [Belyn Hlaalu](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu") at [his farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm") east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

Adisla crawls out of her bed at 6am and spends the first hour of the day wandering around the [farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm"), then sits down and enjoys a one-hour breakfast. At 8am she heads outside and starts working the land. She keeps going for twelve hours until 8pm when she heads back inside for a one-hour dinner. She spends the rest of the evening performing miscellaneous tasks in the farmhouse until she finally goes to bed at midnight.

She wears a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a5 "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") to defend herself and a copy of the [Hlaalu Farmhouse Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farmhouse_Key "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farmhouse Key"). Besides those, she also has a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") in her inventory.

## Dialogue

Speaking to Adisla will have her provide a few comments about herself:

:   *"Starting to get too old to work all day, but hopefully Master Hlaalu will let me slow down a bit."*
:   *"Every now and then someone from the city comes by. Think they aren't used to seeing a Nord working for a Dark Elf."*
:   *"Better to work in the cold than in the heat, I say. Though some sun would be nice."*

## Conversations

Adisla and Belyn

Adisla will talk with her employer, Belyn, on a few occasions. One will have Adisla ask him about a wheat shipment:

:   **Adisla**: *"I was wondering if you had ordered the shipment of that frostwheat, sir."*
:   **Belyn**: *"Yes, but that fool [Endario](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthus_Endario "Skyrim:Orthus Endario") can't get it in. I'll thrash him when I get back to the city, don't you worry."*
:   **Adisla**: *"I wasn't wanting to get anyone in trouble, sir. Just wanting to get the new planting started, is all."*
:   **Belyn**: *"Yes, wouldn't want to miss the lush summer we have ahead."*

In another conversation between the two, Belyn will order Adisla to perform repairs around the farm, and criticize her resource usage:

:   **Belyn**: *"Make sure the back fence is repaired. I swear I saw some [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in nibbling the leaves yesterday. "*
:   **Adisla**: *"Oh, no skeevers out here, sir. They can't stand the cold."*
:   **Belyn**: *"Maybe, but the way you burn through all that wood to keep the cabin toasty, they might mistake this place for [Elsweyr](/wiki/Lore:Elsweyr "Lore:Elsweyr")."*
:   **Adisla**: *"Sorry, sir. These old bones do like a bit of warmth in the evening. There's no need to make fun."*
:   **Belyn**: *"You just need to remember that there's a war on, and firewood isn't cheap these days."*

In another, Belyn will ask her about [Captain Lonely-Gale](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Lonely-Gale "Skyrim:Captain Lonely-Gale"):

:   **Belyn**: *"So have you ever actually spoken to Captain Lonely-Gale?"*
:   **Adisla**: *"By the gods, he's just a retired ship's captain."*
:   **Belyn**: *"Maybe to you, but he's just so... his story is..."*
:   **Adisla**: *"He's just a guard captain. And not a very good one, at that."*

# Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli

## Overview
